### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Arquitetura de Microsserviços

## 1. Documento de Arquitetura (ADR-001)

```
# ADR-001: Arquitetura de Microsserviços V11
Data: 2024-01-15
Status: Aceita
Autores: Tech Lead + Especialista Infra + Especialista Backend

## CONTEXTO:
A V10 do DIYAPP evoluiu para uma arquitetura monolítica que está enfrentando:
1. Acoplamento excessivo entre módulos
2. Dificuldade de deploy independente
3. Escalabilidade limitada por componente
4. Time-to-market lento para novas features
5. Falhas em um módulo afetam todo o sistema

## DECISÃO:
Adotar arquitetura de microsserviços com os seguintes princípios:
1. 6 serviços independentes com bounded contexts claros
2. Comunicação síncrona via gRPC para operações críticas
3. Comunicação assíncrona via Apache Kafka para eventos de domínio
4. API Gateway único para clientes externos
5. Cada serviço com seu próprio banco de dados
6. Containerização com Docker e orquestração via Kubernetes

## OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:
- Opção A: Monólito modularizado - Prós: Simples deploy, debugging fácil. Contras: Escalabilidade limitada, acoplamento.
- Opção B: Microsserviços completos - Prós: Escalabilidade independente, resiliência. Contras: Complexidade operacional, latência.
- Opção C: Arquitetura híbrida (microsserviços + monólito) - Prós: Transição gradual. Contras: Gerenciamento duplo.

Opção escolhida: B - Justificativa: O DIYAPP precisa escalar para 100k usuários ativos com 99.9% uptime. Microsserviços oferecem isolamento de falhas e permitem times autônomos por serviço.

## CONSEQUÊNCIAS:
Positivas:
- Deploy independente por serviço
- Escalabilidade granular
- Stack tecnológica adequada por domínio
- Resiliência (falha em um serviço não derruba o sistema)

Negativas:
- Complexidade de debugging distribuído
- Overhead de comunicação entre serviços
- Gerenciamento de consistência eventual
- Monitoramento distribuído necessário

Riscos:
- Latência de rede entre serviços
- Versionamento de APIs precisa de coordenação
- Mitigação: Implementar circuit breakers, service mesh e contrato de versionamento

## REVISÃO: 2024-04-15
```

## 2. Especificação de Serviços

```yaml
# services-architecture.yaml
version: 'v11'
services:
  api-gateway:
    domain: Edge
    stack: Node.js + Express + TypeScript
    port: 3000
    responsibilities:
      - Routing
      - Rate limiting
      - Authentication
      - Request/Response transformation
    database: None
    communication:
      - gRPC client to all services
      - REST for external clients

  auth-service:
    domain: Identity & Access
    stack: Go + Gin + JWT
    port: 50051
    responsibilities:
      - User authentication
      - Token management
      - OAuth2/OIDC integration
      - Role-based access control
    database: PostgreSQL (users, sessions, permissions)
    communication:
      - gRPC server
      - Kafka producer (auth events)

  user-service:
    domain: User Management
    stack: Python + FastAPI
    port: 50052
    responsibilities:
      - User profiles
      - Preferences
      - User search
      - Activity tracking
    database: PostgreSQL (profiles, preferences)
    communication:
      - gRPC server
      - Kafka consumer (auth events)
      - Kafka producer (user events)

  content-service:
    domain: Content Management
    stack: Java + Spring Boot
    port: 50053
    responsibilities:
      - Content creation/editing
      - Version control
      - Templates management
      - Media processing
    database: MongoDB (content, versions, media)
    communication:
      - gRPC server
      - Kafka consumer (user events)
      - Kafka producer (content events)

  workflow-service:
    domain: Business Logic
    stack: Node.js + NestJS + TypeScript
    port: 50054
    responsibilities:
      - Business workflows
      - Rules engine
      - Approval processes
      - Notifications
    database: PostgreSQL (workflows, rules, notifications)
    communication:
      - gRPC server
      - Kafka consumer (content events)
      - Kafka producer (workflow events)

  analytics-service:
    domain: Insights & Reporting
    stack: Python + FastAPI + Celery
    port: 50055
    responsibilities:
      - Data aggregation
      - Real-time analytics
      - Report generation
      - ML model serving
    database: TimescaleDB (metrics, events)
    communication:
      - gRPC server
      - Kafka consumer (all domain events)
```

## 4. Código Base do Serviço Template

```typescript
// services/template-service/src/index.ts
import express from 'express';
import { createServer } from 'http';
import { Server } from '@grpc/grpc-js';
import { Kafka } from 'kafkajs';
import { logger } from './utils/logger';
import { metrics } from './utils/metrics';
import { healthCheck } from './controllers/health';
import { errorHandler } from './middleware/errorHandler';
import { requestLogger } from './middleware/requestLogger';
import { config } from './config';
import { initDatabase } from './database';
import { initGRPC } from './grpc';
import { initKafka } from './kafka';

class Service {
  private app: express.Application;
  private httpServer: any;
  private grpcServer: Server;
  private kafkaClient: Kafka;

  constructor() {
    this.app = express();
    this.setupMiddleware();
    this.setupRoutes();
    this.setupErrorHandling();
  }

  private setupMiddleware(): void {
    this.app.use(express.json());
    this.app.use(requestLogger);
    this.app.use(metrics.middleware());
  }

  private setupRoutes(): void {
    this.app.get('/health', healthCheck);
    this.app.get('/metrics', metrics.endpoint());
    
    // Service-specific routes
    this.app.use('/api/v1', require('./routes/api').router);
  }

  private setupErrorHandling(): void {
    this.app.use(errorHandler);
  }

  async start(): Promise<void> {
    try {
      // Initialize dependencies
      await initDatabase();
      this.grpcServer = await initGRPC();
      this.kafkaClient = await initKafka();

      // Start HTTP server
      this.httpServer = createServer(this.app);
      this.httpServer.listen(config.httpPort, () => {
        logger.info(`HTTP server listening on port ${config.httpPort}`);
      });

      // Start gRPC server
      this.grpcServer.bindAsync(
        `0.0.0.0:${config.grpcPort}`,
        ServerCredentials.createInsecure(),
        (error, port) => {
          if (error) {
            logger.error('Failed to start gRPC server', { error });
            process.exit(1);
          }
          logger.info(`gRPC server listening on port ${port}`);
        }
      );

      // Graceful shutdown
      process.on('SIGTERM', this.gracefulShutdown.bind(this));
      process.on('SIGINT', this.gracefulShutdown.bind(this));

    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to start service', { error });
      process.exit(1);
    }
  }

  async gracefulShutdown(): Promise<void> {
    logger.info('Starting graceful shutdown...');
    
    // Close HTTP server
    if (this.httpServer) {
      this.httpServer.close(() => {
        logger.info('HTTP server closed');
      });
    }

    // Close gRPC server
    if (this.grpcServer) {
      this.grpcServer.tryShutdown(() => {
        logger.info('gRPC server closed');
      });
    }

    // Close Kafka connections
    if (this.kafkaClient) {
      await this.kafkaClient.disconnect();
      logger.info('Kafka connections closed');
    }

    // Close database connections
    await this.closeDatabase();
    
    logger.info('Graceful shutdown completed');
    process.exit(0);
  }

  private async closeDatabase(): Promise<void> {
    // Implementation depends on database client
  }
}

// Start service
const service = new Service();
service.start().catch((error) => {
  logger.error('Service failed to start', { error });
  process.exit(1);
});
```

## 5. Definição gRPC (Protocol Buffers)

```protobuf
// shared/protos/auth/v1/auth.proto
syntax = "proto3";

package diyapp.auth.v1;

import "google/protobuf/timestamp.proto";

service AuthService {
  rpc Login(LoginRequest) returns (LoginResponse);
  rpc ValidateToken(ValidateTokenRequest) returns (ValidateTokenResponse);
  rpc RefreshToken(RefreshTokenRequest) returns (RefreshTokenResponse);
  rpc Logout(LogoutRequest) returns (LogoutResponse);
}

message LoginRequest {
  string email = 1;
  string password = 2;
  string client_id = 3;
}

message LoginResponse {
  string access_token = 1;
  string refresh_token = 2;
  int32 expires_in = 3;
  string token_type = 4;
  User user = 5;
}

message ValidateTokenRequest {
  string token = 1;
}

message ValidateTokenResponse {
  bool valid = 1;
  User user = 2;
  repeated string permissions = 3;
}

message User {
  string id = 1;
  string email = 2;
  string name = 3;
  repeated string roles = 4;
  google.protobuf.Timestamp created_at = 5;
}
```

## 6. Dockerfile Template

```dockerfile
# services/template-service/Dockerfile
FROM node:18-alpine AS builder

WORKDIR /app

# Install dependencies
COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm ci --only=production

# Copy source
COPY . .

# Build TypeScript
RUN npm run build

# Production image
FROM node:18-alpine

WORKDIR /app

# Install runtime dependencies
RUN apk add --no-cache tini

# Copy built application
COPY --from=builder /app/dist ./dist
COPY --from=builder /app/node_modules ./node_modules
COPY --from=builder /app/package.json ./

# Create non-root user
RUN addgroup -g 1001 -S nodejs && \
    adduser -S nodejs -u 1001

USER nodejs

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=3s --start-period=5s --retries=3 \
  CMD node -e "require('http').get('http://localhost:3000/health', (r) => {process.exit(r.statusCode === 200 ? 0 : 1)})"

# Start application
ENTRYPOINT ["/sbin/tini", "--"]
CMD ["node", "dist/index.js"]
```

## 7. Kubernetes Deployment Template

```yaml
# infrastructure/k8s/templates/service-deployment.yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: {{ .Service.Name }}
  namespace: {{ .Namespace }}
  labels:
    app: {{ .Service.Name }}
    version: {{ .Service.Version }}
spec:
  replicas: {{ .Service.Replicas }}
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: {{ .Service.Name }}
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: {{ .Service.Name }}
        version: {{ .Service.Version }}
    spec:
      containers:
      - name: {{ .Service.Name }}
        image: {{ .Registry }}/{{ .Service.Name }}:{{ .Service.Version }}
        ports:
        - containerPort: {{ .Service.HttpPort }}
        - containerPort: {{ .Service.GrpcPort }}
        env:
        - name: NODE_ENV
          value: "production"
        - name: SERVICE_NAME
          value: {{ .Service.Name }}
        - name: POD_NAME
          valueFrom:
            fieldRef:
              fieldPath: metadata.name
        - name: POD_IP
          valueFrom:
            fieldRef:
              fieldPath: status.podIP
        resources:
          requests:
            memory: "128Mi"
            cpu: "100m"
          limits:
            memory: "256Mi"
            cpu: "200m"
        livenessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health
            port: {{ .Service.HttpPort }}
          initialDelaySeconds: 30
          periodSeconds: 10
        readinessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health
            port: {{ .Service.HttpPort }}
          initialDelaySeconds: 5
          periodSeconds: 5
        volumeMounts:
        - name: config
          mountPath: /app/config
      volumes:
      - name: config
        configMap:
          name: {{ .Service.Name }}-config
---
apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: {{ .Service.Name }}
  namespace: {{ .Namespace }}
spec:
  selector:
    app: {{ .Service.Name }}
  ports:
  - name: http
    port: 80
    targetPort: {{ .Service.HttpPort }}
  - name: grpc
    port: 50051
    targetPort: {{ .Service.GrpcPort }}
  type: ClusterIP
```

## 8. CI/CD Pipeline (GitHub Actions)

```yaml
# .github/workflows/ci.yml
name: CI Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main, develop ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main ]

jobs:
  test:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    strategy:
      matrix:
        service: [auth, user, content, workflow, analytics]
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Setup Node.js
      uses: actions/setup-node@v3
      with:
        node-version: '18'
        cache: 'npm'
        cache-dependency-path: services/${{ matrix.service }}/package-lock.json
    
    - name: Install dependencies
      run: npm ci
      working-directory: services/${{ matrix.service }}
    
    - name: Lint
      run: npm run lint
      working-directory: services/${{ matrix.service }}
    
    - name: Unit tests
      run: npm test -- --coverage
      working-directory: services/${{ matrix.service }}
    
    - name: Upload coverage
      uses: codecov/codecov-action@v3
      with:
        file: services/${{ matrix.service }}/coverage/lcov.info
    
    - name: Build
      run: npm run build
      working-directory: services/${{ matrix.service }}
    
    - name: Security scan
      uses: aquasecurity/trivy-action@master
      with:
        scan-type: 'fs'
        scan-ref: 'services/${{ matrix.service }}'
        format: 'sarif'
        output: 'trivy-results.sarif'
    
    - name: Upload security results
      uses: github/codeql-action/upload-sarif@v2
      with:
        sarif_file: 'trivy-results.sarif'

  integration:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: test
    services:
      postgres:
        image: postgres:14
        env:
          POSTGRES_PASSWORD: test
        options: >-
          --health-cmd pg_isready
          --health-interval 10s
          --health-timeout 5s
          --health-retries 5
      kafka:
        image: confluentinc/cp-kafka:latest
        env:
          KAFKA_BROKER_ID: 1
          KAFKA_ZOOKEEPER_CONNECT: localhost:2181
        options: >-
          --health-cmd "kafka-topics --list --bootstrap-server localhost:9092"
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Run integration tests
      run: |
        docker-compose -f docker-compose.test.yml up -d
        npm run test:integration
        docker-compose -f docker-compose.test.yml down
```

### design-tokens/colors.js
```javascript
// Colors utility with WCAG contrast validation
class ColorSystem {
  constructor() {
    this.tokens = {
      primary: {
        50: '#EFF6FF',
        100: '#DBEAFE',
        200: '#BFDBFE',
        300: '#93C5FD',
        400: '#60A5FA',
        500: '#3B82F6',
        600: '#2563EB',
        700: '#1D4ED8',
        800: '#1E40AF',
        900: '#1E3A8A'
      },
      neutral: {
        50: '#F9FAFB',
        100: '#F3F4F6',
        200: '#E5E7EB',
        300: '#D1D5DB',
        400: '#9CA3AF',
        500: '#6B7280',
        600: '#4B5563',
        700: '#374151',
        800: '#1F2937',
        900: '#111827'
      }
    };
  }

  // WCAG contrast ratio calculation
  getContrastRatio(color1, color2) {
    const luminance1 = this.getLuminance(color1);
    const luminance2 = this.getLuminance(color2);
    const brightest = Math.max(luminance1, luminance2);
    const darkest = Math.min(luminance1, luminance2);
    return (brightest + 0.05) / (darkest + 0.05);
  }

  getLuminance(hex) {
    const rgb = this.hexToRgb(hex);
    const [r, g, b] = Object.values(rgb).map(val => {
      val /= 255;
      return val <= 0.03928 ? val / 12.92 : Math.pow((val + 0.055) / 1.055, 2.4);
    });
    return 0.2126 * r + 0.7152 * g + 0.0722 * b;
  }

  hexToRgb(hex) {
    const result = /^#?([a-f\d]{2})([a-f\d]{2})([a-f\d]{2})$/i.exec(hex);
    return result ? {
      r: parseInt(result[1], 16),
      g: parseInt(result[2], 16),
      b: parseInt(result[3], 16)
    } : { r: 0, g: 0, b: 0 };
  }

  // Validate WCAG AA compliance (4.5:1 for normal text)
  validateContrast(foreground, background) {
    const ratio = this.getContrastRatio(foreground, background);
    return {
      ratio: ratio.toFixed(2),
      aaNormal: ratio >= 4.5,
      aaLarge: ratio >= 3,
      aaaNormal: ratio >= 7,
      aaaLarge: ratio >= 4.5
    };
  }

  // Get accessible text color for background
  getAccessibleTextColor(backgroundColor) {
    const whiteContrast = this.getContrastRatio('#FFFFFF', backgroundColor);
    const blackContrast = this.getContrastRatio('#000000', backgroundColor);
    return whiteContrast > blackContrast ? '#FFFFFF' : '#000000';
  }

  // Generate CSS custom properties
  generateCSS() {
    let css = ':root {\n';
    
    // Primary colors
    Object.entries(this.tokens.primary).forEach(([key, value]) => {
      css += `  --color-primary-${key}: ${value};\n`;
    });
    
    // Neutral colors
    Object.entries(this.tokens.neutral).forEach(([key, value]) => {
      css += `  --color-neutral-${key}: ${value};\n`;
    });
    
    css += '}';
    return css;
  }
}

module.exports = ColorSystem;
```

### design-tokens/typography.js
```javascript
// Typography system with accessibility considerations
class TypographySystem {
  constructor() {
    this.scale = {
      xs: { fontSize: '0.75rem', lineHeight: '1.5' },
      sm: { fontSize: '0.875rem', lineHeight: '1.5' },
      base: { fontSize: '1rem', lineHeight: '1.5' },
      lg: { fontSize: '1.125rem', lineHeight: '1.5' },
      xl: { fontSize: '1.25rem', lineHeight: '1.4' },
      '2xl': { fontSize: '1.5rem', lineHeight: '1.4' },
      '3xl': { fontSize: '1.875rem', lineHeight: '1.25' },
      '4xl': { fontSize: '2.25rem', lineHeight: '1.25' }
    };
    
    this.weights = {
      normal: '400',
      medium: '500',
      semibold: '600',
      bold: '700'
    };
  }

  // Calculate minimum font size for readability
  getMinimumSize(viewingDistance = 20) {
    // Based on WCAG: 1/96 inch per foot of viewing distance
    const inchesPerFoot = 1/96;
    const pixelsPerInch = 96;
    return Math.ceil(viewingDistance * inchesPerFoot * pixelsPerInch);
  }

  // Generate typography classes
  generateClasses() {
    let classes = '';
    
    Object.entries(this.scale).forEach(([name, values]) => {
      classes += `.text-${name} {\n`;
      classes += `  font-size: ${values.fontSize};\n`;
      classes += `  line-height: ${values.lineHeight};\n`;
      classes += '}\n\n';
    });
    
    Object.entries(this.weights).forEach(([name, value]) => {
      classes += `.font-${name} {\n`;
      classes += `  font-weight: ${value};\n`;
      classes += '}\n\n';
    });
    
    return classes;
  }

  // Validate line length for optimal readability
  validateLineLength(fontSize, containerWidth) {
    const charsPerLine = containerWidth / (parseFloat(fontSize) * 0.6);
    return {
      chars: Math.floor(charsPerLine),
      optimal: charsPerLine >= 45 && charsPerLine <= 75,
      recommendation: charsPerLine < 45 ? 'Increase container width' : 
                     charsPerLine > 75 ? 'Decrease container width' : 'Optimal'
    };
  }
}

module.exports = TypographySystem;
```

### component-library/buttons/ButtonSystem.js
```javascript
// Button component system with all states
class ButtonSystem {
  constructor() {
    this.variants = {
      primary: {
        base: 'bg-primary-600 text-white',
        hover: 'hover:bg-primary-700',
        focus: 'focus:ring-2 focus:ring-primary-500 focus:ring-offset-2',
        active: 'active:bg-primary-800',
        disabled: 'disabled:bg-primary-300 disabled:cursor-not-allowed'
      },
      secondary: {
        base: 'bg-neutral-200 text-neutral-900',
        hover: 'hover:bg-neutral-300',
        focus: 'focus:ring-2 focus:ring-neutral-500 focus:ring-offset-2',
        active: 'active:bg-neutral-400',
        disabled: 'disabled:bg-neutral-100 disabled:text-neutral-400'
      },
      danger: {
        base: 'bg-error-600 text-white',
        hover: 'hover:bg-error-700',
        focus: 'focus:ring-2 focus:ring-error-500 focus:ring-offset-2',
        active: 'active:bg-error-800',
        disabled: 'disabled:bg-error-300'
      }
    };

    this.sizes = {
      sm: 'px-3 py-1.5 text-sm',
      md: 'px-4 py-2 text-base',
      lg: 'px-6 py-3 text-lg'
    };
  }

  generateButton(variant = 'primary', size = 'md', fullWidth = false) {
    const variantClasses = this.variants[variant];
    const sizeClass = this.sizes[size];
    const widthClass = fullWidth ? 'w-full' : '';
    
    return {
      base: `inline-flex items-center justify-center border border-transparent rounded-md font-medium transition-colors duration-200 ${variantClasses.base} ${sizeClass} ${widthClass}`,
      states: {
        hover: variantClasses.hover,
        focus: variantClasses.focus,
        active: variantClasses.active,
        disabled: variantClasses.disabled
      },
      accessibility: {
        role: 'button',
        tabindex: '0',
        keyboard: 'Space or Enter to activate'
      }
    };
  }

  // Generate button with loading state
  generateLoadingButton() {
    return {
      base: 'relative inline-flex items-center justify-center',
      spinner: 'absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center',
      content: 'invisible',
      spinnerSVG: `<svg class="animate-spin h-5 w-5 text-white" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
        <circle class="opacity-25" cx="12" cy="12" r="10" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="4"></circle>
        <path class="opacity-75" fill="currentColor" d="M4 12a8 8 0 018-8V0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12h4zm2 5.291A7.962 7.962 0 014 12H0c0 3.042 1.135 5.824 3 7.938l3-2.647z"></path>
      </svg>`
    };
  }

  // Generate icon button
  generateIconButton(icon, label) {
    return {
      html: `<button type="button" class="p-2 rounded-full hover:bg-neutral-100 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-primary-500" aria-label="${label}">
        ${icon}
      </button>`,
      accessibility: {
        label: label,
        role: 'button'
      }
    };
  }
}

module.exports = ButtonSystem;
```

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]
Vou implementar o dashboard V11 com foco em performance crítica. Como Dev Frontend Sênior, seguirei rigorosamente os padrões de performance e fidelidade ao design.

```jsx
// src/App.tsx
import React, { Suspense, lazy, useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { DashboardProvider } from './contexts/DashboardContext';
import { PerformanceMonitor } from './components/PerformanceMonitor';
import { ErrorBoundary } from './components/ErrorBoundary';
import { LoadingSkeleton } from './components/LoadingSkeleton';
import { DesignSystemProvider } from './design-system/DesignSystemProvider';
import './App.css';

// Lazy loading de componentes principais
const DashboardLayout = lazy(() => import('./layouts/DashboardLayout'));
const Sidebar = lazy(() => import('./components/Sidebar'));
const Header = lazy(() => import('./components/Header'));

// Web Worker para cálculos pesados
const analyticsWorker = new Worker(
  new URL('./workers/analytics.worker.ts', import.meta.url)
);

function App() {
  const [isWorkerReady, setIsWorkerReady] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    // Inicializar worker
    analyticsWorker.onmessage = (event) => {
      if (event.data.type === 'READY') {
        setIsWorkerReady(true);
      }
    };

    return () => {
      analyticsWorker.terminate();
    };
  }, []);

  return (
    <ErrorBoundary>
      <DesignSystemProvider>
        <DashboardProvider worker={analyticsWorker}>
          <PerformanceMonitor />
          <div className="app" role="application" aria-label="DIYAPP Evolution Dashboard">
            <Suspense fallback={<LoadingSkeleton type="header" />}>
              <Header />
            </Suspense>
            
            <div className="app-content">
              <Suspense fallback={<LoadingSkeleton type="sidebar" />}>
                <Sidebar />
              </Suspense>
              
              <main className="main-content" id="main-content">
                <Suspense fallback={<LoadingSkeleton type="dashboard" />}>
                  <DashboardLayout />
                </Suspense>
              </main>
            </div>
            
            {!isWorkerReady && (
              <div className="worker-loading" aria-live="polite">
                Otimizando cálculos...
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </DashboardProvider>
      </DesignSystemProvider>
    </ErrorBoundary>
  );
}

export default App;
```

```jsx
// src/layouts/DashboardLayout.tsx
import React, { memo, useMemo, useCallback } from 'react';
import { VirtualizedGrid } from '../components/VirtualizedGrid';
import { MetricsCard } from '../components/cards/MetricsCard';
import { ChartContainer } from '../components/charts/ChartContainer';
import { ActivityFeed } from '../components/ActivityFeed';
import { QuickActions } from '../components/QuickActions';
import { useDashboard } from '../hooks/useDashboard';
import { usePerformance } from '../hooks/usePerformance';
import '../styles/DashboardLayout.css';

interface DashboardItem {
  id: string;
  type: 'metric' | 'chart' | 'feed' | 'action';
  title: string;
  dataKey: string;
  colSpan: 1 | 2;
  rowSpan: 1 | 2;
}

const DashboardLayout = memo(() => {
  const { metrics, charts, activities, isLoading } = useDashboard();
  const { markTime } = usePerformance();

  // Marcar tempo de renderização
  useMemo(() => {
    markTime('dashboard-render-start');
  }, [markTime]);

  const dashboardItems: DashboardItem[] = useMemo(() => [
    { id: 'total-users', type: 'metric', title: 'Total Users', dataKey: 'totalUsers', colSpan: 1, rowSpan: 1 },
    { id: 'active-sessions', type: 'metric', title: 'Active Sessions', dataKey: 'activeSessions', colSpan: 1, rowSpan: 1 },
    { id: 'conversion-rate', type: 'metric', title: 'Conversion Rate', dataKey: 'conversionRate', colSpan: 1, rowSpan: 1 },
    { id: 'revenue', type: 'metric', title: 'Revenue', dataKey: 'revenue', colSpan: 1, rowSpan: 1 },
    { id: 'traffic-chart', type: 'chart', title: 'Traffic Overview', dataKey: 'traffic', colSpan: 2, rowSpan: 2 },
    { id: 'revenue-chart', type: 'chart', title: 'Revenue Trends', dataKey: 'revenueChart', colSpan: 2, rowSpan: 1 },
    { id: 'activity-feed', type: 'feed', title: 'Recent Activity', dataKey: 'activities', colSpan: 1, rowSpan: 2 },
    { id: 'quick-actions', type: 'action', title: 'Quick Actions', dataKey: 'actions', colSpan: 1, rowSpan: 1 },
  ], []);

  const renderItem = useCallback((item: DashboardItem) => {
    switch (item.type) {
      case 'metric':
        return (
          <MetricsCard
            key={item.id}
            title={item.title}
            value={metrics[item.dataKey]?.value}
            change={metrics[item.dataKey]?.change}
            isLoading={isLoading}
          />
        );
      case 'chart':
        return (
          <ChartContainer
            key={item.id}
            title={item.title}
            data={charts[item.dataKey]}
            type={item.dataKey === 'traffic' ? 'line' : 'bar'}
            isLoading={isLoading}
          />
        );
      case 'feed':
        return (
          <ActivityFeed
            key={item.id}
            activities={activities}
            isLoading={isLoading}
          />
        );
      case 'action':
        return <QuickActions key={item.id} />;
      default:
        return null;
    }
  }, [metrics, charts, activities, isLoading]);

  return (
    <div className="dashboard-layout" role="region" aria-label="Dashboard content">
      <VirtualizedGrid
        items={dashboardItems}
        renderItem={renderItem}
        columnWidth={280}
        rowHeight={200}
        gap={16}
        overscan={2}
        ariaLabel="Dashboard widgets grid"
      />
    </div>
  );
});

DashboardLayout.displayName = 'DashboardLayout';

export default DashboardLayout;
```

```jsx
// src/components/VirtualizedGrid.tsx
import React, { memo, useRef, useEffect, useState, useCallback } from 'react';
import { useResizeObserver } from '../hooks/useResizeObserver';
import { useScrollPosition } from '../hooks/useScrollPosition';
import '../styles/VirtualizedGrid.css';

interface VirtualizedGridProps<T> {
  items: T[];
  renderItem: (item: T, index: number) => React.ReactNode;
  columnWidth: number;
  rowHeight: number;
  gap: number;
  overscan?: number;
  ariaLabel?: string;
}

export const VirtualizedGrid = memo(<T extends { id: string; colSpan: number; rowSpan: number }>({
  items,
  renderItem,
  columnWidth,
  rowHeight,
  gap,
  overscan = 3,
  ariaLabel = 'Virtualized grid'
}: VirtualizedGridProps<T>) => {
  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const [visibleRange, setVisibleRange] = useState({ start: 0, end: 0 });
  const [containerSize, setContainerSize] = useState({ width: 0, height: 0 });
  
  const { width: containerWidth } = useResizeObserver(containerRef);
  const scrollTop = useScrollPosition(containerRef);

  // Calcular layout de grid
  const { columns, itemPositions } = useMemo(() => {
    if (!containerWidth) return { columns: 0, itemPositions: [] };
    
    const columns = Math.floor((containerWidth + gap) / (columnWidth + gap));
    const positions: Array<{ top: number; left: number; width: number; height: number }> = [];
    
    // Algoritmo de packing simples (poderia usar masonry layout mais avançado)
    let colHeights = new Array(columns).fill(0);
    
    items.forEach(item => {
      const itemColSpan = Math.min(item.colSpan, columns);
      const itemWidth = itemColSpan * columnWidth + (itemColSpan - 1) * gap;
      const itemHeight = item.rowSpan * rowHeight + (item.rowSpan - 1) * gap;
      
      // Encontrar coluna com menor altura
      let targetCol = 0;
      let minHeight = Infinity;
      
      for (let col = 0; col <= columns - itemColSpan; col++) {
        const colHeight = Math.max(...colHeights.slice(col, col + itemColSpan));
        if (colHeight < minHeight) {
          minHeight = colHeight;
          targetCol = col;
        }
      }
      
      positions.push({
        top: minHeight,
        left: targetCol * (columnWidth + gap),
        width: itemWidth,
        height: itemHeight
      });
      
      // Atualizar alturas das colunas
      for (let col = targetCol; col < targetCol + itemColSpan; col++) {
        colHeights[col] = minHeight + itemHeight + gap;
      }
    });
    
    return { columns, itemPositions: positions };
  }, [items, containerWidth, columnWidth, rowHeight, gap]);

  // Calcular itens visíveis
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!containerRef.current || itemPositions.length === 0) return;
    
    const containerHeight = containerRef.current.clientHeight;
    const startIdx = itemPositions.findIndex(pos => 
      pos.top + pos.height >= scrollTop - (overscan * rowHeight)
    );
    const endIdx = itemPositions.findIndex(pos => 
      pos.top >= scrollTop + containerHeight + (overscan * rowHeight)
    );
    
    setVisibleRange({
      start: Math.max(0, startIdx),
      end: endIdx === -1 ? items.length : Math.min(items.length, endIdx)
    });
  }, [scrollTop, itemPositions, overscan, rowHeight, items.length]);

  const handleKeyDown = useCallback((e: React.KeyboardEvent) => {
    // Navegação por teclado na grid
    const activeElement = document.activeElement;
    if (!activeElement || !containerRef.current) return;
    
    const items = containerRef.current.querySelectorAll('[data-grid-item]');
    const currentIndex = Array.from(items).indexOf(activeElement);
    
    switch (e.key) {
      case 'ArrowRight':
        e.preventDefault();
        if (currentIndex < items.length - 1) {
          (items[currentIndex + 1] as HTMLElement).focus();
        }
        break;
      case 'ArrowLeft':
        e.preventDefault();
        if (currentIndex > 0) {
          (items[currentIndex - 1] as HTMLElement).focus();
        }
        break;
      case 'Home':
        e.preventDefault();
        (items[0] as HTMLElement).focus();
        break;
      case 'End':
        e.preventDefault();
        (items[items.length - 1] as HTMLElement).focus();
        break;
    }
  }, []);

  return (
    <div
      ref={containerRef}
      className="virtualized-grid"
      role="grid"
      aria-label={ariaLabel}
      aria-rowcount={Math.ceil(items.length / columns)}
      aria-colcount={columns}
      tabIndex={0}
      onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
      style={{
        height: '100%',
        overflowY: 'auto',
        position: 'relative'
      }}
    >
      <div
        className="grid-content"
        style={{
          height: itemPositions.length > 0 
            ? Math.max(...itemPositions.map(p => p.top + p.height)) 
            : 0
        }}
      >
        {items.slice(visibleRange.start, visibleRange.end).map((item, index) => {
          const absoluteIndex = visibleRange.start + index;
          const position = itemPositions[absoluteIndex];
          
          if (!position) return null;
          
          return (
            <div
              key={item.id}
              data-grid-item
              className="grid-item"
              role="gridcell"
              aria-rowindex={Math.floor(absoluteIndex / columns) + 1}
              aria-colindex={(absoluteIndex % columns) + 1}
              tabIndex={0}
              style={{
                position: 'absolute',
                top: `${position.top}px`,
                left: `${position.left}px`,
                width: `${position.width}px`,
                height: `${position.height}px`,
                transition: 'transform 0.2s ease'
              }}
            >
              {renderItem(item, absoluteIndex)}
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
});

VirtualizedGrid.displayName = 'VirtualizedGrid';
```

```typescript
// src/workers/analytics.worker.ts
// Web Worker para processamento pesado de analytics

interface WorkerMessage {
  type: string;
  payload?: any;
}

// Tipos de mensagens
type MessageType = 
  | 'CALCULATE_METRICS'
  | 'PROCESS_CHART_DATA'
  | 'AGGREGATE_ACTIVITIES'
  | 'READY';

// Funções pesadas que serão executadas no worker
const calculateMetrics = (rawData: any[]) => {
  // Cálculos complexos de métricas
  const startTime = performance.now();
  
  const metrics = {
    totalUsers: {
      value: rawData.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.users || 0), 0),
      change: 0
    },
    activeSessions: {
      value: rawData.filter(item => item.isActive).length,
      change: 0
    },
    conversionRate: {
      value: rawData.length > 0 
        ? (rawData.filter(item => item.converted).length / rawData.length) * 100 
        : 0,
      change: 0
    },
    revenue: {
      value: rawData.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.revenue || 0), 0),
      change: 0
    }
  };
  
  // Calcular mudanças percentuais (simulação)
  if (rawData.length > 1) {
    const half = Math.floor(rawData.length / 2);
    const firstHalf = rawData.slice(0, half);
    const secondHalf = rawData.slice(half);
    
    const firstHalfRevenue = firstHalf.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.revenue || 0), 0);
    const secondHalfRevenue = secondHalf.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.revenue || 0), 0);
    
    if (firstHalfRevenue > 0) {
      metrics.revenue.change = ((secondHalfRevenue - firstHalfRevenue) / firstHalfRevenue) * 100;
    }
  }
  
  const endTime = performance.now();
  console.log(`Metrics calculation took ${endTime - startTime}ms`);
  
  return metrics;
};

const processChartData = (rawData: any[], type: 'line' | 'bar') => {
  // Processamento pesado de dados para gráficos
  const startTime = performance.now();
  
  const processedData = rawData.map((item, index) => ({
    timestamp: item.timestamp || new Date(Date.now() - (rawData.length - index) * 3600000).toISOString(),
    value: item.value || Math.random() * 100,
    category: item.category || `Category ${index % 5}`
  }));
  
  // Agregação por período para otimização de renderização
  const aggregated = processedData.reduce((acc, item) => {
    const date = new Date(item.timestamp);
    const hour = date.getHours();
    const key = `${date.getDate()}-${hour}`;
    
    if (!acc[key]) {
      acc[key] = {
        timestamp: new Date(date.getFullYear(), date.getMonth(), date.getDate(), hour).toISOString(),
        values: [],
        count: 0
      };
    }
    
    acc[key].values.push(item.value);
    acc[key].count++;
    return acc;
  }, {} as Record<string, any>);
  
  const result = Object.values(aggregated).map((item: any) => ({
    x: item.timestamp,
    y: item.values.reduce((sum: number, val: number) => sum + val, 0) / item.count
  }));
  
  const endTime = performance.now();
  console.log(`Chart data processing took ${endTime - startTime}ms`);
  
  return result;
};

// Handler principal do worker
self.onmessage = (e: MessageEvent<WorkerMessage>) => {
  const { type, payload } = e.data;
  
  try {
    switch (type) {
      case 'CALCULATE_METRICS':
        const metrics = calculateMetrics(payload);
        self.postMessage({ type: 'METRICS_CALCULATED', payload: metrics });
        break;
        
      case 'PROCESS_CHART_DATA':
        const chartData = processChartData(payload.data, payload.type);
        self.postMessage({ 
          type: 'CHART_DATA_PROCESSED', 
          payload: { 
            key: payload.key,
            data: chartData 
          }
        });
        break;
        
      case 'AGGREGATE_ACTIVITIES':
        // Processamento de atividades em lote
        const activities = payload.map((item: any) => ({
          id: item.id,
          user: item.user,
          action: item.action,
          timestamp: item.timestamp,
          details: item.details
        }));
        self.postMessage({ 
          type: 'ACTIVITIES_AGGREGATED', 
          payload: activities 
        });
        break;
        
      default:
        console.warn('Unknown message type:', type);
    }
  } catch (error) {
    self.postMessage({ 
      type: 'ERROR', 
      payload: { 
        message: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error',
        originalType: type 
      }
    });
  }
};

// Notificar que o worker está pronto
self.postMessage({ type: 'READY' });
```

// src/hooks/useDashboard.ts
import {

## 2. docker-compose.yml

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # Redis for caching and Bull queues
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-redis
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes --requirepass ${REDIS_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # PostgreSQL for persistent storage
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-postgres
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: ${POSTGRES_DB}
      POSTGRES_USER: ${POSTGRES_USER}
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./init.sql:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/init.sql
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U ${POSTGRES_USER}"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # API Gateway
  api-gateway:
    build:
      context: .
      dockerfile: docker/Dockerfile.api-gateway
    container_name: diyapp-api-gateway
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - PORT=3000
      - REDIS_URL=redis://:${REDIS_PASSWORD}@redis:6379
      - POSTGRES_URL=postgres://${POSTGRES_USER}:${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/${POSTGRES_DB}
      - JWT_SECRET=${JWT_SECRET}
      - API_KEY=${API_KEY}
    depends_on:
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
    volumes:
      - ./logs:/app/logs
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3000/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Agent Orchestrator
  agent-orchestrator:
    build:
      context: .
      dockerfile: docker/Dockerfile.agent-orchestrator
    container_name: diyapp-agent-orchestrator
    ports:
      - "3001:3001"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - PORT=3001
      - REDIS_URL=redis://:${REDIS_PASSWORD}@redis:6379
      - POSTGRES_URL=postgres://${POSTGRES_USER}:${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/${POSTGRES_DB}
      - GATEWAY_URL=http://api-gateway:3000
    depends_on:
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
      api-gateway:
        condition: service_healthy
    volumes:
      - ./logs:/app/logs
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3001/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Memory Manager
  memory-manager:
    build:
      context: .
      dockerfile: docker/Dockerfile.memory-manager
    container_name: diyapp-memory-manager
    ports:
      - "3002:3002"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - PORT=3002
      - REDIS_URL=redis://:${REDIS_PASSWORD}@redis:6379
      - POSTGRES_URL=postgres://${POSTGRES_USER}:${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/${POSTGRES_DB}
      - OPENAI_API_KEY=${OPENAI_API_KEY}
      - GATEWAY_URL=http://api-gateway:3000
    depends_on:
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
      api-gateway:
        condition: service_healthy
    volumes:
      - ./logs:/app/logs
      - ./embeddings:/app/embeddings
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3002/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Bull Dashboard (Queue Monitoring)
  bull-dashboard:
    image: beequeue/dashboard:latest
    container_name: diyapp-bull-dashboard
    ports:
      - "3003:3003"
    environment:
      - REDIS_URI=redis://:${REDIS_PASSWORD}@redis:6379
    depends_on:
      - redis
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

networks:
  diyapp-network:
    driver: bridge

volumes:
  redis_data:
  postgres_data:

## 3. Configuração Compartilhada

### src/shared/config/index.js
```javascript
require('dotenv').config();

const config = {
  // Server
  nodeEnv: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development',
  port: parseInt(process.env.PORT || '3000', 10),
  
  // Redis
  redis: {
    url: process.env.REDIS_URL || 'redis://localhost:6379',
    password: process.env.REDIS_PASSWORD,
    tls: process.env.REDIS_TLS === 'true',
    maxRetriesPerRequest: 3,
    enableReadyCheck: false,
  },
  
  // PostgreSQL
  postgres: {
    url: process.env.POSTGRES_URL || 'postgres://postgres:postgres@localhost:5432/diyapp',
    pool: {
      max: 20,
      min: 5,
      acquire: 30000,
      idle: 10000,
    },
  },
  
  // JWT
  jwt: {
    secret: process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'your-super-secret-jwt-key-change-in-production',
    expiresIn: '24h',
    algorithm: 'HS256',
  },
  
  // API Gateway
  gateway: {
    url: process.env.GATEWAY_URL || 'http://localhost:3000',
    apiKey: process.env.API_KEY,
    timeout: 10000, // 10 seconds
  },
  
  // Rate Limiting
  rateLimit: {
    windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
    max: 100, // limit each IP to 100 requests per windowMs
    standardHeaders: true,
    legacyHeaders: false,
  },
  
  // Circuit Breaker
  circuitBreaker: {
    timeout: 3000, // 3 seconds
    errorThresholdPercentage: 50,
    resetTimeout: 30000, // 30 seconds
  },
  
  // Retry Policy
  retry: {
    maxAttempts: 3,
    delay: 1000, // 1 second
    backoffFactor: 2,
  },
  
  // Logging
  logging: {
    level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
    file: {
      maxSize: '20m',
      maxFiles: '14d',
      datePattern: 'YYYY-MM-DD',
    },
  },
  
  // Monitoring
  monitoring: {
    metrics: {
      enabled: true,
      port: 9090,
      path: '/metrics',
    },
    health: {
      enabled: true,
      path: '/health',
    },
  },
  
  // Memory Manager
  memory: {
    embeddingModel: 'text-embedding-ada-002',
    maxTokens: 8191,
    similarityThreshold: 0.7,
    cacheTtl: 3600, // 1 hour
  },
  
  // Agent Orchestrator
  orchestrator: {
    maxConcurrentAgents: 10,
    agentTimeout: 30000, // 30 seconds
    taskQueue: 'agent-tasks',
    resultQueue: 'agent-results',
  },
};

// Validate required environment variables
const requiredEnvVars = ['JWT_SECRET', 'API_KEY'];
if (config.nodeEnv === 'production') {
  requiredEnvVars.forEach((envVar) => {
    if (!process.env[envVar]) {
      throw new Error(`Missing required environment variable: ${envVar}`);
    }
  });
}

module.exports = config;
```

### src/shared/config/redis.js
```javascript
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const config = require('./index');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');

class RedisClient {
  constructor() {
    this.client = null;
    this.publisher = null;
    this.subscriber = null;
    this.isConnected = false;
  }

  async connect() {
    if (this.isConnected) return;

    try {
      // Main client for commands
      this.client = new Redis(config.redis.url, {
        maxRetriesPerRequest: config.redis.maxRetriesPerRequest,
        enableReadyCheck: config.redis.enableReadyCheck,
        retryStrategy: (times) => {
          const delay = Math.min(times * 50, 2000);
          return delay;
        },
      });

      // Separate publisher for pub/sub
      this.publisher = new Redis(config.redis.url);

      // Separate subscriber for pub/sub
      this.subscriber = new Redis(config.redis.url);

      // Event listeners
      this.client.on('connect', () => {
        logger.info('Redis client connected');
      });

      this.client.on('error', (error) => {
        logger.error('Redis client error:', error);
      });

      this.client.on('close', () => {
        logger.warn('Redis client connection closed');
        this.isConnected = false;
      });

      this.client.on('reconnecting', () => {
        logger.info('Redis client reconnecting...');
      });

      // Wait for connection
      await this.client.ping();
      this.isConnected = true;
      logger.info('Redis connection established');

    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to connect to Redis:', error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async disconnect() {
    if (this.client) {
      await this.client.quit();
    }
   

### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Data Lake para Telemetria de Agentes

## Arquitetura do Data Lake

```
data-lake/
├── ingestion/           # Ingestão de logs e métricas
├── storage/            # PostgreSQL/TimescaleDB + Elasticsearch
├── transformation/     # Processamento e enriquecimento
├── monitoring/         # Dashboards e alertas
└── orchestration/      # Pipeline orchestration
```

## 1. Schema do Banco de Dados (PostgreSQL/TimescaleDB)

### 1.1. Tabela de Métricas de Agente (TimescaleDB)

```sql
-- schema/metrics.sql
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS timescaledb;

-- Tabela principal de métricas de execução
CREATE TABLE agent_execution_metrics (
    time TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    agent_id VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    squad_id VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    execution_id UUID NOT NULL,
    task_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    
    -- Métricas de performance
    execution_time_ms INTEGER NOT NULL,
    cpu_usage_percent DECIMAL(5,2),
    memory_usage_mb INTEGER,
    token_count INTEGER,
    cost_usd DECIMAL(10,6),
    
    -- Métricas de qualidade
    success BOOLEAN NOT NULL,
    error_code VARCHAR(50),
    error_message TEXT,
    retry_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Métricas de negócio
    input_tokens INTEGER,
    output_tokens INTEGER,
    model_used VARCHAR(50),
    provider VARCHAR(50),
    
    -- Metadados
    hostname VARCHAR(100),
    version VARCHAR(20),
    environment VARCHAR(20),
    
    -- Índices
    PRIMARY KEY (time, agent_id, execution_id)
);

-- Converter para hypertable do TimescaleDB
SELECT create_hypertable('agent_execution_metrics', 'time');

-- Índices para queries frequentes
CREATE INDEX idx_agent_metrics_agent_id ON agent_execution_metrics(agent_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_agent_metrics_squad_id ON agent_execution_metrics(squad_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_agent_metrics_success ON agent_execution_metrics(success);
CREATE INDEX idx_agent_metrics_task_type ON agent_execution_metrics(task_type);

-- Tabela de agregações diárias
CREATE TABLE agent_daily_aggregates (
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    agent_id VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    squad_id VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    
    -- Contagens
    total_executions BIGINT NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    successful_executions BIGINT NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    failed_executions BIGINT NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Tempos
    avg_execution_time_ms DECIMAL(10,2),
    p95_execution_time_ms DECIMAL(10,2),
    p99_execution_time_ms DECIMAL(10,2),
    
    -- Custos
    total_cost_usd DECIMAL(12,6),
    avg_cost_per_execution DECIMAL(10,6),
    
    -- Tokens
    total_input_tokens BIGINT,
    total_output_tokens BIGINT,
    avg_tokens_per_execution DECIMAL(10,2),
    
    -- Última execução
    last_execution_time TIMESTAMPTZ,
    
    PRIMARY KEY (date, agent_id, squad_id)
);

-- Tabela de health check dos agentes
CREATE TABLE agent_health_status (
    agent_id VARCHAR(100) PRIMARY KEY,
    squad_id VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    last_heartbeat TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    status VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL CHECK (status IN ('healthy', 'degraded', 'unhealthy')),
    consecutive_failures INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    avg_response_time_ms DECIMAL(10,2),
    last_error TEXT,
    metadata JSONB
);
```

### 1.2. Tabelas de Suporte

```sql
-- schema/support_tables.sql
-- Tabela de configuração de alertas
CREATE TABLE alert_configurations (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    alert_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    alert_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL CHECK (alert_type IN ('threshold', 'anomaly', 'absence')),
    agent_id VARCHAR(100),
    squad_id VARCHAR(50),
    metric_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    operator VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL CHECK (operator IN ('>', '<', '=', '!=', '>=', '<=')),
    threshold_value DECIMAL(20,6),
    window_minutes INTEGER,
    cooldown_minutes INTEGER DEFAULT 5,
    severity VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL CHECK (severity IN ('info', 'warning', 'critical')),
    notification_channels JSONB,
    enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Tabela de alertas disparados
CREATE TABLE triggered_alerts (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    alert_configuration_id INTEGER REFERENCES alert_configurations(id),
    triggered_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    resolved_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    metric_value DECIMAL(20,6),
    threshold_value DECIMAL(20,6),
    status VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL CHECK (status IN ('triggered', 'acknowledged', 'resolved')),
    acknowledged_by VARCHAR(100),
    acknowledged_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    resolution_notes TEXT
);

-- Tabela de retenção de dados
CREATE TABLE data_retention_policies (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    table_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    retention_days INTEGER NOT NULL,
    compression_enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    archive_enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    archive_location VARCHAR(500),
    last_cleanup TIMESTAMPTZ,
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Inserir políticas padrão
INSERT INTO data_retention_policies (table_name, retention_days) VALUES
('agent_execution_metrics', 90),
('triggered_alerts', 365),
('agent_daily_aggregates', 730);
```

## 2. Configuração do Elasticsearch para Logs

```yaml
# elasticsearch/config/logs-index-template.yaml
apiVersion: elasticsearch.k8s.elastic.co/v1
kind: Elasticsearch
metadata:
  name: diyapp-logs
spec:
  version: 8.10.0
  nodeSets:
  - name: hot
    count: 3
    config:
      node.roles: ["data_hot", "ingest", "remote_cluster_client"]
      xpack.ml.enabled: false
    podTemplate:
      spec:
        containers:
        - name: elasticsearch
          resources:
            requests:
              memory: 4Gi
              cpu: 2
            limits:
              memory: 8Gi
              cpu: 4
  - name: warm
    count: 2
    config:
      node.roles: ["data_warm"]
    podTemplate:
      spec:
        containers:
        - name: elasticsearch
          resources:
            requests:
              memory: 2Gi
              cpu: 1
            limits:
              memory: 4Gi
              cpu: 2
```

```json
// elasticsearch/mappings/agent-logs-mapping.json
{
  "index_patterns": ["agent-logs-*"],
  "template": {
    "settings": {
      "number_of_shards": 3,
      "number_of_replicas": 1,
      "index.lifecycle.name": "agent-logs-policy",
      "index.lifecycle.rollover_alias": "agent-logs"
    },
    "mappings": {
      "dynamic": "strict",
      "properties": {
        "@timestamp": {
          "type": "date"
        },
        "agent_id": {
          "type": "keyword"
        },
        "squad_id": {
          "type": "keyword"
        },
        "execution_id": {
          "type": "keyword"
        },
        "log_level": {
          "type": "keyword"
        },
        "message": {
          "type": "text",
          "fields": {
            "keyword": {
              "type": "keyword",
              "ignore_above": 256
            }
          }
        },
        "component": {
          "type": "keyword"
        },
        "trace_id": {
          "type": "keyword"
        },
        "span_id": {
          "type": "keyword"
        },
        "duration_ms": {
          "type": "long"
        },
        "http_status": {
          "type": "integer"
        },
        "error_code": {
          "type": "keyword"
        },
        "stack_trace": {
          "type": "text"
        },
        "metadata": {
          "type": "object",
          "dynamic": true
        },
        "host": {
          "properties": {
            "hostname": {
              "type": "keyword"
            },
            "ip": {
              "type": "ip"
            },
            "container_id": {
              "type": "keyword"
            }
          }
        },
        "labels": {
          "type": "keyword"
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
```

## 3. Sistema de Ingestão de Alta Performance

```python
# ingestion/agent_telemetry_ingestor.py
import asyncio
import json
import time
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Dict, List, Optional
import psycopg2
from psycopg2.extras import execute_batch
from psycopg2.pool import ThreadedConnectionPool
import aioredis
from elasticsearch import AsyncElasticsearch
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
import uuid
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor
import logging
from prometheus_client import Counter, Histogram, Gauge

# Métricas Prometheus
INGESTED_METRICS = Counter('agent_metrics_ingested_total', 'Total metrics ingested')
INGESTED_LOGS = Counter('agent_logs_ingested_total', 'Total logs ingested')
INGESTION_LATENCY = Histogram('ingestion_latency_seconds', 'Ingestion latency')
BUFFER_SIZE = Gauge('ingestion_buffer_size', 'Current buffer size')
DB_CONNECTIONS = Gauge('db_connections_active', 'Active database connections')

@dataclass
class AgentMetric:
    agent_id: str
    squad_id: str
    execution_id: str
    task_type: str
    execution_time_ms: int
    cpu_usage_percent: Optional[float] = None
    memory_usage_mb: Optional[int] = None
    token_count: Optional[int] = None
    cost_usd: Optional[float] = None
    success: bool = True
    error_code: Optional[str] = None
    error_message: Optional[str] = None
    retry_count: int = 0
    input_tokens: Optional[int] = None
    output_tokens: Optional[int] = None
    model_used: Optional[str] = None
    provider: Optional[str] = None
    hostname: Optional[str] = None
    version: Optional[str] = None
    environment: Optional[str] = None

@dataclass
class AgentLog:
    agent_id: str
    squad_id: str
    execution_id: str
    log_level: str
    message: str
    component: str
    trace_id: Optional[str] = None
    span_id: Optional[str] = None
    duration_ms: Optional[int] = None
    http_status: Optional[int] = None
    error_code: Optional[str] = None
    stack_trace: Optional[str] = None
    metadata: Optional[Dict] = None
    hostname: Optional[str] = None
    ip: Optional[str] = None
    container_id: Optional[str] = None
    labels: Optional[List[str]] = None

class TelemetryIngestor:
    def __init__(self, config: Dict):
        self.config = config
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
        
        # Connection pools
        self.db_pool = None
        self.redis_pool = None
        self.es_client = None
        
        # Buffers para batch processing
        self.metrics_buffer = []
        self.logs_buffer = []
        self.buffer_lock = asyncio.Lock()
        
        # Configurações
        self.batch_size = config.get('batch_size', 1000)
        self.flush_interval = config.get('flush_interval', 5)  # segundos
        self.max_buffer_size = config.get('max_buffer_size', 10000)
        
        # Executor para operações bloqueantes
        self.thread_pool = ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=10)
        
        # Estatísticas
        self.stats = {
            'metrics_ingested': 0,
            'logs_ingested': 0,
            'last_flush': datetime.utcnow()
        }
    
    async def initialize(self):
        """Inicializa conexões com os bancos de dados"""
        try:
            # PostgreSQL/TimescaleDB connection pool
            self.db_pool = ThreadedConnectionPool(
                minconn=5,
                maxconn=20,
                host=self.config['postgres']['host'],
                port=self.config['postgres']['port'],
                database=self.config['postgres']['database'],
                user=self.config['postgres']['user'],
                password=self.config['postgres']['password']
            )
            
            # Redis para buffer e cache
            self.redis_pool = await aioredis.create_redis_pool(
                f"redis://{self.config['redis']['host']}:{self.config['redis']['port']}",
                minsize=5,
                maxsize=20
            )
            
            # Elasticsearch client
            self.es_client = AsyncElasticsearch(
                hosts=[self.config['elasticsearch']['host']],
                basic_auth=(
                    self.config['elasticsearch']['user'],
                    self.config['elasticsearch']['password']
                ),
                max_retries=3,
                retry_on_timeout=True
            )
            
            self.logger.info("Telemetry ingestor initialized successfully")
            
            # Inicia task de flush periódico
            asyncio.create_task(self._periodic_flush())
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Failed to initialize ingestor: {e}")
            raise
    
    async def ingest_metric(self, metric: AgentMetric):
        """Ingere uma métrica de agente"""
        async with self.buffer_lock:
            self.metrics_buffer.append(metric)
            INGESTED_METRICS.inc()
            BUFFER_SIZE.set(len(self.metrics_buffer) + len(self.logs_buffer))
            
            # Flush se buffer atingir tamanho máximo
            if len(self.metrics_buffer) >= self.batch_size:
                await self._flush_metrics()
    
    async def ingest_log(self, log: AgentLog):
        """Ingere um log de agente"""
        async with self.buffer_lock:
            self.logs_buffer.append(log)
            INGESTED_LOGS.inc()
            BUFFER_SIZE.set(len(self.metrics_buffer) + len(self.logs_buffer))
            
            # Flush se buffer atingir tamanho máximo
            if len(self.logs_buffer) >= self.batch_size:
                await self._flush_logs()
    
    async def _periodic_flush(self):
        """Flush periódico dos buffers"""
        while True:
            await asyncio.sleep(self.flush_interval)
            
            async with self.buffer_lock:
                if self.metrics_buffer:
                    await self._flush_metrics()
                if self.logs_buffer:
                    await self._flush_logs()
                
                self.stats['last_flush'] = datetime.utcnow()
    
    async def _flush_metrics(self):
        """Flush das métricas para PostgreSQL"""
        if not self.metrics_buffer:
            return
        
        batch = self.metrics_buffer[:self.batch_size]
        self.metrics_buffer = self.metrics_buffer[self.batch_size:]
        
        try:
            start_time = time.time()
            
            # Converter para formato de tupla para batch insert
            records = []
            for metric in batch:
                records.append((
                    datetime.utcnow(),
                    metric.agent_id,
                    metric.squad_id,
                    uuid.UUID(metric.execution_id),
                    metric.task_type,
                    metric.execution_time_ms,
                    metric.cpu_usage_percent,
                    metric.memory_usage_mb,
                    metric.token_count,
                    metric.cost_usd,
                    metric.success,
                    metric.error_code,
                    metric.error_message,
                    metric.retry_count,
                    metric.input_tokens,
                    metric.output_tokens,
                    metric.model_used,
                    metric.provider,
                    metric.hostname,
                    metric.version,
                    metric.environment
                ))
            
            # Executar batch insert
            conn = self.db_pool.getconn()
            try:
                cursor = conn.cursor()
                execute_batch(cursor, """
                    INSERT INTO agent_execution_metrics (
                        time, agent_id, squad_id, execution_id, task_type,
                        execution_time_ms, cpu_usage_percent, memory_usage_mb,
                        token_count, cost_usd, success, error_code, error_message,
                        retry_count, input_tokens, output_tokens, model_used,
                        provider, hostname, version, environment
                    ) VALUES (%s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s)
                """, records)
                conn.commit()
                
                self.stats['metrics_ingested'] += len(batch)
                INGESTION_LATENCY.observe(time.time() - start_time)
                
                self.logger.debug(f"Flushed {len(batch)} metrics to PostgreSQL")
                
            finally:
                self.db_pool.putconn(conn)
                
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Failed to flush metrics: {e}")
            # Re-add to buffer for retry
            async with self.buffer_lock:
                self.metrics_buffer.extend(batch)
    
    async def _flush_logs(self):
        """Flush dos logs para Elasticsearch"""
        if not self.logs_buffer:
            return
        
        batch = self.logs_buffer[:self.batch_size]
        self.logs_buffer = self.logs_buffer[self.batch_size:]
        
        try:
           

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Arquitetura de Microsserviços

## 1. Documento de Arquitetura (ADR-001)

### Architecture Decision Record - ADR-001: Arquitetura de Microsserviços V11

**Data:** 2024-01-15  
**Status:** Aceita  
**Autores:** Tech Lead V11, Especialista Infra, Especialista Backend  

**CONTEXTO:**
DIYAPP evoluiu de uma aplicação monolítica para uma plataforma distribuída com múltiplos serviços especializados. A versão V11 precisa suportar:
- Escalabilidade horizontal independente por domínio
- Deploy contínuo sem downtime
- Comunicação assíncrona entre serviços
- Observabilidade unificada
- 100% de autonomia operacional

**DECISÃO:**
Adotar arquitetura de microsserviços com os seguintes padrões:
1. **Comunicação síncrona:** gRPC para comunicação service-to-service com baixa latência
2. **Comunicação assíncrona:** Apache Kafka para eventos de domínio
3. **Service Mesh:** Istio para gerenciamento de tráfego, segurança e observabilidade
4. **Banco de dados:** Database-per-service com PostgreSQL para dados transacionais
5. **Cache distribuído:** Redis Cluster
6. **API Gateway:** Kong com plugins customizados
7. **Monitoramento:** Prometheus + Grafana + Jaeger

**OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:**

**Opção A: REST + RabbitMQ**
- Prós: Simples, amplamente adotado, fácil debugging
- Contras: Overhead de serialização JSON, sem contrato forte, versionamento complexo

**Opção B: gRPC + Kafka**
- Prós: Alto desempenho (HTTP/2 + Protobuf), contrato forte via Protobuf, streaming bidirecional
- Contras: Curva de aprendizado, tooling menos maduro para debugging

**Opção C: GraphQL + NATS**
- Prós: Flexibilidade no frontend, schema federation
- Contras: Complexidade no backend, over-fetching em serviços internos

**Opção escolhida: B** - Justificativa: Performance crítica para comunicação interna, contratos fortes previnem breaking changes, Kafka oferece melhor escalabilidade para eventos.

**CONSEQUÊNCIAS:**
**Positivas:**
- Alta performance em comunicações internas
- Contratos explícitos via Protobuf
- Escalabilidade horizontal independente
- Observabilidade unificada via service mesh

**Negativas:**
- Complexidade operacional aumentada
- Necessidade de expertise em gRPC e Kafka
- Overhead de serialização/deserialização Protobuf

**Riscos:**
1. **Latência na comunicação:** Mitigação com circuit breakers e timeouts configurados
2. **Perda de eventos:** Mitigação com confirmações do Kafka e dead letter queues
3. **Versionamento de contratos:** Mitigação com backward compatibility no Protobuf

**REVISÃO:** 2024-04-15 (3 meses para reavaliar métricas de performance)

---

### 3. Código Base do Microsserviço

#### 3.1. Protobuf Definitions

**src/proto/diyapp/v1/user.proto:**
```proto
syntax = "proto3";

package diyapp.v1;

import "google/protobuf/timestamp.proto";

service UserService {
  rpc GetUser(GetUserRequest) returns (UserResponse);
  rpc CreateUser(CreateUserRequest) returns (UserResponse);
  rpc UpdateUser(UpdateUserRequest) returns (UserResponse);
  rpc ListUsers(ListUsersRequest) returns (ListUsersResponse);
}

message User {
  string id = 1;
  string email = 2;
  string name = 3;
  UserStatus status = 4;
  google.protobuf.Timestamp created_at = 5;
  google.protobuf.Timestamp updated_at = 6;
}

enum UserStatus {
  ACTIVE = 0;
  INACTIVE = 1;
  SUSPENDED = 2;
}

message GetUserRequest {
  string user_id = 1;
}

message CreateUserRequest {
  string email = 1;
  string name = 2;
  string password = 3;
}

message UpdateUserRequest {
  string user_id = 1;
  optional string name = 2;
  optional UserStatus status = 3;
}

message ListUsersRequest {
  int32 page = 1;
  int32 limit = 2;
  optional UserStatus status = 3;
}

message ListUsersResponse {
  repeated User users = 1;
  int32 total = 2;
  int32 page = 3;
  int32 total_pages = 4;
}

message UserResponse {
  User user = 1;
}
```

#### 3.2. User Service Implementation

**src/services/user-service/src/server.js:**
```javascript
const grpc = require('@grpc/grpc-js');
const protoLoader = require('@grpc/proto-loader');
const path = require('path');
const { Kafka } = require('kafkajs');
const { Pool } = require('pg');
const winston = require('winston');

// Configuração
const PROTO_PATH = path.join(__dirname, '../../../proto/diyapp/v1/user.proto');
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 50051;
const DB_CONFIG = {
  host: process.env.DB_HOST || 'localhost',
  port: parseInt(process.env.DB_PORT) || 5432,
  database: process.env.DB_NAME || 'diyapp_users',
  user: process.env.DB_USER || 'postgres',
  password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD || 'postgres',
  max: 20,
  idleTimeoutMillis: 30000,
  connectionTimeoutMillis: 2000,
};

// Logger
const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  format: winston.format.combine(
    winston.format.timestamp(),
    winston.format.json()
  ),
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.Console(),
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/user-service.log' })
  ],
});

// Database connection
const pool = new Pool(DB_CONFIG);

// Kafka setup
const kafka = new Kafka({
  clientId: 'user-service',
  brokers: (process.env.KAFKA_BROKERS || 'localhost:9092').split(','),
  ssl: process.env.KAFKA_SSL === 'true',
  sasl: process.env.KAFKA_SASL_USERNAME ? {
    mechanism: 'plain',
    username: process.env.KAFKA_SASL_USERNAME,
    password: process.env.KAFKA_SASL_PASSWORD,
  } : undefined,
});

const producer = kafka.producer();
const consumer = kafka.consumer({ groupId: 'user-service-group' });

// Load protobuf
const packageDefinition = protoLoader.loadSync(PROTO_PATH, {
  keepCase: true,
  longs: String,
  enums: String,
  defaults: true,
  oneofs: true,
});

const protoDescriptor = grpc.loadPackageDefinition(packageDefinition);
const diyapp = protoDescriptor.diyapp.v1;

// Service implementation
class UserService {
  constructor() {
    this.users = new Map();
  }

  async getUser(call, callback) {
    try {
      logger.info('GetUser request', { userId: call.request.user_id });
      
      const result = await pool.query(
        'SELECT * FROM users WHERE id = $1 AND deleted_at IS NULL',
        [call.request.user_id]
      );
      
      if (result.rows.length === 0) {
        return callback({
          code: grpc.status.NOT_FOUND,
          message: 'User not found'
        });
      }
      
      const user = result.rows[0];
      const response = {
        user: {
          id: user.id,
          email: user.email,
          name: user.name,
          status: user.status,
          created_at: {
            seconds: Math.floor(user.created_at.getTime() / 1000),
            nanos: (user.created_at.getTime() % 1000) * 1000000
          },
          updated_at: {
            seconds: Math.floor(user.updated_at.getTime() / 1000),
            nanos: (user.updated_at.getTime() % 1000) * 1000000
          }
        }
      };
      
      callback(null, response);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('GetUser error', { error: error.message });
      callback({
        code: grpc.status.INTERNAL,
        message: 'Internal server error'
      });
    }
  }

  async createUser(call, callback) {
    const transaction = await pool.connect();
    
    try {
      await transaction.query('BEGIN');
      
      logger.info('CreateUser request', { email: call.request.email });
      
      // Check if user exists
      const existingUser = await transaction.query(
        'SELECT id FROM users WHERE email = $1 AND deleted_at IS NULL',
        [call.request.email]
      );
      
      if (existingUser.rows.length > 0) {
        await transaction.query('ROLLBACK');
        return callback({
          code: grpc.status.ALREADY_EXISTS,
          message: 'User already exists'
        });
      }
      
      // Create user
      const result = await transaction.query(
        `INSERT INTO users (email, name, password_hash, status) 
         VALUES ($1, $2, crypt($3, gen_salt('bf')), 'ACTIVE')
         RETURNING id, email, name, status, created_at, updated_at`,
        [call.request.email, call.request.name, call.request.password]
      );
      
      const user = result.rows[0];
      
      // Publish event
      await producer.send({
        topic: 'user-events',
        messages: [{
          key: user.id,
          value: JSON.stringify({
            event_type: 'USER_CREATED',
            user_id: user.id,
            email: user.email,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
          })
        }]
      });
      
      await transaction.query('COMMIT');
      
      const response = {
        user: {
          id: user.id,
          email: user.email,
          name: user.name,
          status: user.status,
          created_at: {
            seconds: Math.floor(user.created_at.getTime() / 1000),
            nanos: (user.created_at.getTime() % 1000) * 1000000
          },
          updated_at: {
            seconds: Math.floor(user.updated_at.getTime() / 1000),
            nanos: (user.updated_at.getTime() % 1000) * 1000000
          }
        }
      };
      
      callback(null, response);
    } catch (error) {
      await transaction.query('ROLLBACK');
      logger.error('CreateUser error', { error: error.message });
      callback({
        code: grpc.status.INTERNAL,
        message: 'Internal server error'
      });
    } finally {
      transaction.release();
    }
  }

  async updateUser(call, callback) {
    const transaction = await pool.connect();
    
    try {
      await transaction.query('BEGIN');
      
      logger.info('UpdateUser request', { 
        userId: call.request.user_id,
        updates: call.request
      });
      
      // Build dynamic update query
      const updates = [];
      const values = [];
      let paramCount = 1;
      
      if (call.request.name !== undefined) {
        updates.push(`name = $${paramCount}`);
        values.push(call.request.name);
        paramCount++;
      }
      
      if (call.request.status !== undefined) {
        updates.push(`status = $${paramCount}`);
        values.push(call.request.status);
        paramCount++;
      }
      
      if (updates.length === 0) {
        await transaction.query('ROLLBACK');
        return callback({
          code: grpc.status.INVALID_ARGUMENT,
          message: 'No fields to update'
        });
      }
      
      updates.push(`updated_at = NOW()`);
      values.push(call.request.user_id);
      
      const query = `
        UPDATE users 
        SET ${updates.join(', ')}
        WHERE id = $${paramCount} AND deleted_at IS NULL
        RETURNING id, email, name, status, created_at, updated_at
      `;
      
      const result = await transaction.query(query, values);
      
      if (result.rows.length === 0) {
        await transaction.query('ROLLBACK');
        return callback({
          code: grpc.status.NOT_FOUND,
          message: 'User not found'
        });
      }
      
      const user = result.rows[0];
      
      // Publish event
      await producer.send({
        topic: 'user-events',
        messages: [{
          key: user.id,
          value: JSON.stringify({
            event_type: 'USER_UPDATED',
            user_id: user.id,
            updates: call.request,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
          })
        }]
      });
      
      await transaction.query('COMMIT');
      
      const response = {
        user: {
          id: user.id,
          email: user.email,
          name: user.name,
          status: user.status,
          created_at: {
            seconds: Math.floor(user.created_at.getTime() / 1000),
            nanos: (user.created_at.getTime() % 1000) * 1000000
          },
          updated_at: {
            seconds: Math.floor(user.updated_at.getTime() / 1000),
            nanos: (user.updated_at.getTime() % 1000) * 1000000
          }
        }
      };
      
      callback(null, response);
    } catch (error) {
      await transaction.query('ROLLBACK');
      logger.error('UpdateUser error', { error: error.message });
      callback({
        code: grpc.status.INTERNAL,
        message: 'Internal server error'
      });
    } finally {
      transaction.release();
    }
  }

  async listUsers(call, callback) {
    try {
      logger.info('ListUsers request', { 
        page: call.request.page,
        limit: call.request.limit
      });
      
      const page = call.request.page || 1;
      const limit = call.request.limit || 20;
      const offset = (page - 1) * limit;
      
      let query = 'SELECT * FROM users WHERE deleted_at IS NULL';
      let countQuery = 'SELECT COUNT(*) FROM users WHERE deleted_at IS NULL';
      const params = [];
      let paramCount = 1;
      
      if (call.request.status !== undefined) {
        query += ` AND status = $${paramCount}`;
        countQuery += ` AND status = $${paramCount}`;
        params.push(call.request.status);
        paramCount++;
      }
      
      query += ` ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]

## 1. Design Tokens (design-tokens.json)

      "primary": {

        "600": "#475569",
        "700": "#334155",
        "800": "#1e293b",
        "900": "#0f172a"
      },

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]
Vou implementar o dashboard V11 com foco em performance crítica (<2s carregamento, Lighthouse >=95). Usarei React com virtualização, lazy loading e Web Workers.

```jsx
// package.json
{
  "name": "diyapp-dashboard-v11",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "type": "module",
  "scripts": {
    "dev": "vite",

    "preview": "vite preview",
    "test": "vitest",
    "lint": "eslint . --ext ts,tsx --report-unused-disable-directives --max-warnings 0"
  },
  "dependencies": {
    "react": "^18.2.0",
    "react-dom": "^18.2.0",
    "react-virtual": "^3.0.0-beta.40",

```ts
// vite.config.ts
import { defineConfig } from 'vite'
import react from '@vitejs/plugin-react'

export default defineConfig({
  plugins: [react()],
  build: {
    target: 'es2020',
    rollupOptions: {
      output: {
        manualChunks: {
          'react-vendor': ['react', 'react-dom'],
          'charts-vendor': ['recharts'],
          'utils-vendor': ['date-fns', 'clsx']
        }
      }
    }
  },
  server: {
    port: 3000
  }
})
