```ts
// src/design-system/tokens.ts
export const tokens = {
  colors: {
    primary: {
      50: '#eff6ff',
      100: '#dbeafe',
      200: '#bfdbfe',
      300: '#93c5fd',
      400: '#60a5fa',
      500: '#3b82f6',
      600: '#2563eb',
      700: '#1d4ed8',
      800: '#1e40af',
      900: '#1e3a8a'
    },
    neutral: {
      50: '#fafafa',
      100: '#f5f5f5',
      200: '#e5e5e5',
      300: '#d4d4d4',
      400: '#a3a3a3',
      500: '#737373',
      600: '#525252',
      700: '#404040',
      800: '#262626',
      900: '#171717'
    },
    success: {
      500: '#10b981',
      600: '#059669'
    },
    warning: {
      500: '#f59e0b',
      600: '#d97706'
    },
    error: {
      500: '#ef4444',
      600: '#dc2626'
    }
  },
  spacing: {
    0: '0',
    1: '0.25rem',
    2: '0.5rem',
    3: '0.75rem',
    4: '1rem',
    5: '1.25rem',
    6: '1.5rem',
    8: '2rem',
    10: '2.5rem',
    12: '3rem',
    16: '4rem',
    20: '5rem'
  },
  typography: {
    fontFamily: {
      sans: "'Inter', -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, sans-serif",
      mono: "'JetBrains Mono', 'Courier New', monospace"
    },
    fontSize: {
      xs: '0.75rem',
      sm: '0.875rem',
      base: '1rem',
      lg: '1.125rem',
      xl: '1.25rem',
      '2xl': '1.5rem',
      '3xl': '1.875rem',
      '4xl': '2.25rem'
    },
    fontWeight: {
      normal: '400',
      medium: '500',
      semibold: '600',
      bold: '700'
    }
  },
  borderRadius: {
    sm: '0.125rem',
    base: '0.25rem',
    md: '0.375rem',
    lg: '0.5rem',
    xl: '0.75rem',
    '2xl': '1rem',
    full: '9999px'
  },
  shadows: {
    sm: '0 1px 2px 0 rgb(0 0 0 / 0.05)',
    base: '0 1px 3px 0 rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1), 0 1px 2px -1px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
    md: '0 4px 6px -1px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1), 0 2px 4px -2px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
    lg: '0 10px 15px -3px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1), 0 4px 6px -4px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)'
  }
} as const

export type ColorToken = keyof typeof tokens.colors
export type SpacingToken = keyof typeof tokens.spacing
```

```tsx
// src/components/Layout/DashboardLayout.tsx
import React, { Suspense, lazy } from 'react'
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens'
import { Sidebar } from './Sidebar'
import { Header } from './Header'
import { LoadingFallback } from '../Feedback/LoadingFallback'

const PerformanceMonitor = lazy(() => 
  import('../Performance/PerformanceMonitor').then(m => ({ default: m.PerformanceMonitor }))
)

interface DashboardLayoutProps {
  children: React.ReactNode
}

export const DashboardLayout: React.FC<DashboardLayoutProps> = ({ children }) => {
  return (
    <div style={{
      display: 'flex',
      minHeight: '100vh',
      backgroundColor: tokens.colors.neutral[50],
      fontFamily: tokens.typography.fontFamily.sans
    }}>
      <Sidebar />
      
      <div style={{
        flex: 1,
        display: 'flex',
        flexDirection: 'column',
        marginLeft: '250px'
      }}>
        <Header />
        
        <main style={{
          flex: 1,
          padding: tokens.spacing[6],
          overflowY: 'auto'
        }}>
          <Suspense fallback={<LoadingFallback />}>
            {children}
          </Suspense>
        </main>
        
        <Suspense fallback={null}>
          <PerformanceMonitor />
        </Suspense>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}
```

```tsx
// src/components/Layout/Sidebar.tsx
import React from 'react'
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens'
import { 
  LayoutDashboard, 
  BarChart3, 
  Users, 
  Settings, 
  FileText,
  Bell,
  HelpCircle
} from 'lucide-react'

const menuItems = [
  { icon: LayoutDashboard, label: 'Dashboard', active: true },
  { icon: BarChart3, label: 'Analytics' },
  { icon: Users, label: 'Users' },
  { icon: FileText, label: 'Documents' },
  { icon: Bell, label: 'Notifications' },
  { icon: Settings, label: 'Settings' },
  { icon: HelpCircle, label: 'Help' }
]

export const Sidebar: React.FC = () => {
  return (
    <aside style={{
      width: '250px',
      backgroundColor: 'white',
      borderRight: `1px solid ${tokens.colors.neutral[200]}`,
      position: 'fixed',
      height: '100vh',
      overflowY: 'auto'
    }}>
      <div style={{
        padding: tokens.spacing[6],
        borderBottom: `1px solid ${tokens.colors.neutral[200]}`
      }}>
        <h1 style={{
          fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize['2xl'],
          fontWeight: tokens.typography.fontWeight.bold,
          color: tokens.colors.primary[700],
          margin: 0
        }}>
          DIYAPP V11
        </h1>
        <p style={{
          fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.sm,
          color: tokens.colors.neutral[500],
          marginTop: tokens.spacing[1]
        }}>
          Autonomous Dashboard
        </p>
      </div>
      
      <nav style={{ padding: tokens.spacing[4] }}>
        <ul style={{ listStyle: 'none', padding: 0, margin: 0 }}>
          {menuItems.map((item) => {
            const Icon = item.icon
            return (
              <li key={item.label} style={{ marginBottom: tokens.spacing[2] }}>
                <button
                  style={{
                    display: 'flex',
                    alignItems: 'center',
                    width: '100%',
                    padding: `${tokens.spacing[3]} ${tokens.spacing[4]}`,
                    backgroundColor: item.active ? tokens.colors.primary[50] : 'transparent',
                    color: item.active ? tokens.colors.primary[700] : tokens.colors.neutral[700],
                    border: 'none',
                    borderRadius: tokens.borderRadius.lg,
                    fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.sm,
                    fontWeight: tokens.typography.fontWeight.medium,
                    cursor: 'pointer',
                    transition: 'all 0.2s',
                    textAlign: 'left'
                  }}
                  onMouseEnter={(e) => {
                    if (!item.active) {
                      e.currentTarget.style.backgroundColor = tokens.colors.neutral[100]
                    }
                  }}
                  onMouseLeave={(e) => {
                    if (!item.active) {
                      e.currentTarget.style.backgroundColor = 'transparent'
                    }
                  }}
                >
                  <Icon size={20} style={{ marginRight: tokens.spacing[3] }} />
                  {item.label}
                </button>
              </li>
            )
          })}
        </ul>
      </nav>
    </aside>
  )
}
```

```tsx
// src/components/Layout/Header.tsx
import React from 'react'
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens'
import { Search, Bell, User } from 'lucide-react'

export const Header: React.FC = () => {
  return (
    <header style={{
      backgroundColor: 'white',
      borderBottom: `1px solid ${tokens.colors.neutral[200]}`,
      padding: `${tokens.spacing[4]} ${tokens.spacing[6]}`,
      display: 'flex',
      alignItems: 'center',
      justifyContent: 'space-between'
    }}>
      <div style={{ position: 'relative', flex: 1, maxWidth: '400px' }}>
        <Search 
          size={20} 
          style={{
            position: 'absolute',
            left: tokens.spacing[3],
            top: '50%',
            transform: 'translateY(-50%)',
            color: tokens.colors.neutral[400]
          }} 
        />
        <input
          type="search"
          placeholder="Search dashboard..."
          style={{
            width: '100%',
            padding: `${tokens.spacing[2]} ${tokens.spacing[2]} ${tokens.spacing[2]} ${tokens.spacing[10]}`,
            border: `1px solid ${tokens.colors.neutral[300]}`,
            borderRadius: tokens.borderRadius.lg,
            fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.sm,
            backgroundColor: tokens.colors.neutral[50],
            outline: 'none',
            transition: 'border-color 0.2s'
          }}
          onFocus={(e) => {
            e.target.style.borderColor = tokens.colors.primary[500]
          }}
          onBlur={(e) => {
            e.target.style.borderColor = tokens.colors.neutral[300]
          }}
        />
      </div>
      
      <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: tokens.spacing[4] }}>
        <button
          style={{
            position: 'relative',
            backgroundColor: 'transparent',
            border: 'none',
            padding: tokens.spacing[2],
            borderRadius: tokens.borderRadius.full,
            cursor: 'pointer',
            color: tokens.colors.neutral[600]
          }}
          aria-label="Notifications"
        >
          <Bell size={20} />
          <span style={{
            position: 'absolute',
            top: '4px',
            right: '4px',
            width: '8px',
            height: '8px',
            backgroundColor: tokens.colors.error[500],
            borderRadius: '50%',
            border: `2px solid white`
          }} />
        </button>
        
        <div style={{
          display: 'flex',
          alignItems: 'center',
          gap: tokens.spacing[3],
          padding: `${tokens.spacing[2]} ${tokens.spacing[4]}`,
          backgroundColor: tokens.colors.neutral[50],
          borderRadius: tokens.borderRadius.lg
        }}>
          <div style={{
            width: '32px',
            height: '32px',
            borderRadius: '50%',
            backgroundColor: tokens.colors.primary[100],
            display: 'flex',
            alignItems: 'center',
            justifyContent: 'center',
            color: tokens.colors.primary[600]
          }}>
            <User size={16} />
          </div>
          <div>
            <p style={{
              fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.sm,
              fontWeight: tokens.typography.fontWeight.medium,
              margin: 0,
              color: tokens.colors.neutral[800]
            }}>
              John Developer
            </p>
            <p style={{
              fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.xs,
              margin: 0,
              color: tokens.colors.neutral[500]
            }}>
              Admin
            </p>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </header>
  )
}
```

```tsx
// src/components/Data/DataGrid.tsx
import React, { useMemo } from 'react'
import { FixedSizeList as List } from 'react-window'
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens'

interface DataItem {
  id: string
  name: string
  status: 'active' | 'inactive' | 'pending'
  value: number
  date: string
}

interface DataGridProps {
  data: DataItem[]
  height?: number
}

const StatusBadge: React.FC<{ status: DataItem['status'] }> = ({ status }) => {
  const config = {
    active: { color: tokens.colors.success[500], bg: tokens.colors.success[50] },
    inactive: { color: tokens.colors.neutral[500], bg: tokens.colors.neutral[100] },
    pending: { color: tokens.colors.warning[500], bg: tokens.colors.warning[50] }
  }[status]

  return (
    <span style={{
      padding: `${tokens.spacing[1]} ${tokens.spacing[3]}`,
      backgroundColor: config.bg,
      color: config.color,
      borderRadius: tokens.borderRadius.full,
      fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.xs,
      fontWeight: tokens.typography.fontWeight.medium
    }}>
      {status}
    </span>
  )
}

const Row: React.FC<{ index: number; style: React.CSSProperties; data: DataItem[] }> = ({ index, style, data }) => {
  const item = data[index]
  
  return (
    <div style={{
      ...style,
      display: 'flex',
      alignItems: 'center',
      padding: `${tokens.spacing[4]} ${tokens.spacing[6]}`,
      borderBottom: `1px solid ${tokens.colors.neutral[200]}`,
      backgroundColor: index % 2 === 0 ? 'white' : tokens.colors.neutral[50]
    }}>
      <div style={{ flex: 2, minWidth: 0 }}>
        <p style={{
          margin: 0,
          fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.sm,
          fontWeight: tokens.typography.fontWeight.medium,
          color: tokens.colors.neutral[900]
        }}>
          {item.name}
        </p>
      </div>
      <div style={{ flex: 1, minWidth: 0 }}>
        <StatusBadge status={item.status} />
      </div>
      <div style={{ flex: 1, minWidth: 0 }}>
        <p style={{
          margin: 0,
          fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.sm,
          color: tokens.colors.neutral[700]
        }}>
          ${item.value.toLocaleString()}
        </p>
      </div>
      <div style={{ flex: 1, minWidth: 0 }}>
        <p style={{
          margin: 0,
          fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.sm,
          color: tokens.colors.neutral[600]
        }}>
          {item.date}
        </p>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
Vou construir os serviços core do DIYAPP Evolution V11 com foco em estabilidade, performance e observabilidade. Implementarei uma arquitetura robusta com Node.js, Redis, Bull e documentação completa.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```

version: '3.8'

services:
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-redis
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 3

  api-gateway:
    build: .
    container_name: diyapp-api-gateway
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379
      - AGENT_ORCHESTRATOR_URL=http://agent-orchestrator:3001
      - MEMORY_MANAGER_URL=http://memory-manager:3002
    depends_on:
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3000/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3

  agent-orchestrator:
    build: .
    container_name: diyapp-agent-orchestrator

**src/shared/config.js**
```javascript
const Joi = require('joi');

const envSchema = Joi.object({
  NODE_ENV: Joi.string()
    .valid('development', 'production', 'test')
    .default('development'),
  
  PORT: Joi.number()
    .default(3000),
  
  REDIS_URL: Joi.string()
    .uri()
    .default('redis://localhost:6379'),
  
  LOG_LEVEL: Joi.string()
    .valid('error', 'warn', 'info', 'debug')
    .default('info'),
  
  API_VERSION: Joi.string()
    .default('v1'),
  
  RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS: Joi.number()
    .default(900000),
  
  RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS: Joi.number()
    .default(100),
  
  CIRCUIT_BREAKER_TIMEOUT: Joi.number()
    .default(10000),
  
  CIRCUIT_BREAKER_THRESHOLD: Joi.number()
    .default(5),
  
  CIRCUIT_BREAKER_RESET_TIMEOUT: Joi.number()
    .default(30000),
  
  MEMORY_TTL: Joi.number()
    .default(86400000),
  
  MEMORY_MAX_ITEMS: Joi.number()
    .default(10000)
}).unknown();

const { value: envVars, error } = envSchema.validate(process.env);

if (error) {
  throw new Error(`Config validation error: ${error.message}`);
}

module.exports = {
  env: envVars.NODE_ENV,
  port: envVars.PORT,
  redisUrl: envVars.REDIS_URL,
  logLevel: envVars.LOG_LEVEL,
  apiVersion: envVars.API_VERSION,
  rateLimit: {
    windowMs: envVars.RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS,
    max: envVars.RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS
  },
  circuitBreaker: {
    timeout: envVars.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_TIMEOUT,
    threshold: envVars.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_THRESHOLD,
    resetTimeout: envVars.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_RESET_TIMEOUT
  },
  memory: {
    ttl: envVars.MEMORY_TTL,
    maxItems: envVars.MEMORY_MAX_ITEMS
  }
};
```

**src/shared/logger.js**
```javascript
const winston = require('winston');
const config = require('./config');

const { combine, timestamp, json, errors } = winston.format;

const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: config.logLevel,
  format: combine(
    errors({ stack: true }),
    timestamp(),
    json()
  ),
  defaultMeta: { service: 'diyapp-core' },
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.Console({
      format: combine(
        timestamp({ format: 'YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss' }),
        winston.format.printf(({ timestamp, level, message, service, correlationId, ...meta }) => {
          const metaStr = Object.keys(meta).length ? ` ${JSON.stringify(meta)}` : '';
          return `${timestamp} [${service}] ${level.toUpperCase()}: ${message}${metaStr}`;
        })
      )
    })
  ]
});

// Log stream for Morgan
logger.stream = {
  write: (message) => {
    logger.info(message.trim());
  }
};

module.exports = logger;
```

**src/shared/redis.js**
```javascript
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const logger = require('./logger');
const config = require('./config');

class RedisClient {
  constructor() {
    this.client = new Redis(config.redisUrl, {
      retryStrategy: (times) => {
        const delay = Math.min(times * 50, 2000);
        return delay;
      },
      maxRetriesPerRequest: 3,
      enableReadyCheck: true,
      connectTimeout: 10000
    });

    this.client.on('connect', () => {
      logger.info('Redis connected successfully');
    });

    this.client.on('error', (err) => {
      logger.error('Redis connection error:', { error: err.message });
    });

    this.client.on('close', () => {
      logger.warn('Redis connection closed');
    });
  }

  async get(key) {
    try {
      const value = await this.client.get(key);
      return value ? JSON.parse(value) : null;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Redis get error:', { key, error: error.message });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async set(key, value, ttl = null) {
    try {
      const stringValue = JSON.stringify(value);
      if (ttl) {
        await this.client.setex(key, ttl, stringValue);
      } else {
        await this.client.set(key, stringValue);
      }
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Redis set error:', { key, error: error.message });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async del(key) {
    try {
      await this.client.del(key);
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Redis delete error:', { key, error: error.message });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async exists(key) {
    try {
      const result = await this.client.exists(key);
      return result === 1;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Redis exists error:', { key, error: error.message });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async incr(key) {
    try {
      return await this.client.incr(key);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Redis incr error:', { key, error: error.message });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async expire(key, seconds) {
    try {
      await this.client.expire(key, seconds);
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Redis expire error:', { key, seconds, error: error.message });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async healthCheck() {
    try {
      await this.client.ping();
      return { status: 'healthy', service: 'redis' };
    } catch (error) {
      return { status: 'unhealthy', service: 'redis', error: error.message };
    }
  }

  async disconnect() {
    await this.client.quit();
  }
}

module.exports = new RedisClient();
```

**src/shared/circuitBreaker.js**
```javascript
const CircuitBreaker = require('circuit-breaker-js');
const logger = require('./logger');
const config = require('./config');

class ServiceCircuitBreaker {
  constructor(serviceName) {
    this.serviceName = serviceName;
    
    this.breaker = new CircuitBreaker({
      timeoutDuration: config.circuitBreaker.timeout,
      errorThreshold: config.circuitBreaker.threshold,
      resetTimeout: config.circuitBreaker.resetTimeout,
      onCircuitOpen: (metrics) => {
        logger.warn(`Circuit breaker opened for ${serviceName}`, {
          service: serviceName,
          metrics
        });
      },
      onCircuitClose: (metrics) => {
        logger.info(`Circuit breaker closed for ${serviceName}`, {
          service: serviceName,
          metrics
        });
      }
    });
  }

  async execute(fn, fallback = null) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      this.breaker.run(
        (success, fail) => {
          fn()
            .then((result) => {
              success(result);
              resolve(result);
            })
            .catch((error) => {
              fail(error);
              reject(error);
            });
        },
        (error) => {
          logger.error(`Circuit breaker fallback for ${this.serviceName}`, {
            service: this.serviceName,
            error: error.message
          });
          
          if (fallback) {
            resolve(fallback());
          } else {
            reject(new Error(`Service ${this.serviceName} unavailable`));
          }
        }
      );
    });
  }

  getState() {
    return {
      service: this.serviceName,
      isOpen: this.breaker.isOpen(),
      metrics: this.breaker.metrics
    };
  }
}

module.exports = ServiceCircuitBreaker;
```

    {

  ]

  swaggerDefinition,
  apis: ['./src/**/*.js']
};

## 1. Docker Compose para Infraestrutura

**docker-compose.yml**
```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # TimescaleDB (PostgreSQL com extensões de timeseries)
  timescaledb:
    image: timescale/timescaledb:latest-pg14
    container_name: diyapp-timescaledb
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp_telemetry
      POSTGRES_USER: diyapp_admin
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${TIMESCALE_PASSWORD}
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    volumes:
      - timescale-data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./src/storage/timescale-init.sql:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/init.sql
    command: postgres -c shared_preload_libraries=timescaledb -c max_connections=200
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U diyapp_admin"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  # Elasticsearch para logs
  elasticsearch:
    image: docker.elastic.co/elasticsearch/elasticsearch:8.11.0
    container_name: diyapp-elasticsearch
    environment:
      - discovery.type=single-node
      - xpack.security.enabled=false
      - "ES_JAVA_OPTS=-Xms2g -Xmx2g"
      - cluster.routing.allocation.disk.threshold_enabled=false
    ports:
      - "9200:9200"
    volumes:
      - elastic-data:/usr/share/elasticsearch/data
      - ./src/storage/elasticsearch-mapping.json:/usr/share/elasticsearch/config/mapping.json

## 2. Schema Definitions

**src/storage/schema-definition.sql**
```sql
-- TimescaleDB Schema for Agent Telemetry

-- Enable TimescaleDB extension
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS timescaledb;

-- Raw agent events table (hypertable for time-series)
CREATE TABLE raw_agent_events (
    event_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    agent_id VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    agent_version VARCHAR(20),
    squad_id VARCHAR(50),
    event_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    event_subtype VARCHAR(50),
    
    -- Performance metrics
    execution_time_ms INTEGER,
    memory_usage_mb DECIMAL(10,2),
    cpu_percent DECIMAL(5,2),
    tokens_consumed INTEGER,
    tokens_generated INTEGER,
    
    -- Status and results
    status VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    error_code VARCHAR(50),
    error_message TEXT,
    result_size_bytes INTEGER,
    
    -- Context
    task_id VARCHAR(100),
    user_id VARCHAR(100),
    session_id VARCHAR(100),
    request_id VARCHAR(100),
    
    -- Metadata
    hostname VARCHAR(100),
    ip_address INET,
    user_agent TEXT,
    
    -- Timestamps
    event_timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    processed_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    
    -- Indexes
    INDEX idx_agent_id (agent_id),
    INDEX idx_event_type (event_type),
    INDEX idx_status (status),
    INDEX idx_squad_id (squad_id),
    INDEX idx_event_timestamp (event_timestamp DESC)
);

-- Convert to hypertable with 7-day chunks
SELECT create_hypertable(
    'raw_agent_events', 
    'event_timestamp',
    chunk_time_interval => INTERVAL '7 days',
    if_not_exists => TRUE
);

-- Add compression for older data
ALTER TABLE raw_agent_events SET (
    timescaledb.compress,
    timescaledb.compress_orderby = 'event_timestamp DESC',
    timescaledb.compress_segmentby = 'agent_id, event_type'
);

-- Agent performance aggregates (materialized view)
CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW agent_performance_hourly
WITH (timescaledb.continuous) AS
SELECT
    time_bucket('1 hour', event_timestamp) AS bucket,
    agent_id,
    agent_version,
    squad_id,
    event_type,
    
    -- Counts
    COUNT(*) AS total_events,
    COUNT(CASE WHEN status = 'success' THEN 1 END) AS success_count,
    COUNT(CASE WHEN status = 'error' THEN 1 END) AS error_count,
    COUNT(CASE WHEN status = 'timeout' THEN 1 END) AS timeout_count,
    
    -- Performance percentiles
    percentile_agg(execution_time_ms) AS execution_time_stats,
    percentile_agg(memory_usage_mb) AS memory_usage_stats,
    percentile_agg(cpu_percent) AS cpu_usage_stats,
    
    -- Token usage
    SUM(tokens_consumed) AS total_tokens_consumed,
    SUM(tokens_generated) AS total_tokens_generated,
    AVG(tokens_consumed) AS avg_tokens_per_request,
    
    -- Error analysis
    MODE() WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY error_code) AS most_common_error,
    COUNT(DISTINCT error_code) AS distinct_error_codes
    
FROM raw_agent_events
GROUP BY bucket, agent_id, agent_version, squad_id, event_type
WITH NO DATA;

-- Refresh policy for materialized view
SELECT add_continuous_aggregate_policy('agent_performance_hourly',
    start_offset => INTERVAL '1 hour',
    end_offset => INTERVAL '5 minutes',
    schedule_interval => INTERVAL '5 minutes'
);

-- System health metrics table
CREATE TABLE system_health_metrics (
    metric_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    metric_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    metric_value DECIMAL(15,4) NOT NULL,
    metric_unit VARCHAR(20),
    
    -- Dimensions
    hostname VARCHAR(100),
    service_name VARCHAR(50),
    squad_id VARCHAR(50),
    
    -- Tags for filtering
    tags JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    
    -- Timestamps
    collected_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    
    INDEX idx_metric_name (metric_name),
    INDEX idx_collected_at (collected_at DESC),
    INDEX idx_squad_service (squad_id, service_name)
);

-- Convert to hypertable
SELECT create_hypertable(
    'system_health_metrics',
    'collected_at',
    chunk_time_interval => INTERVAL '1 day',
    if_not_exists => TRUE
);

-- Retention policies
SELECT add_retention_policy('raw_agent_events', INTERVAL '90 days');
SELECT add_retention_policy('system_health_metrics', INTERVAL '30 days');

-- User for application access
CREATE USER diyapp_app WITH PASSWORD 'AppPassword123!';
GRANT CONNECT ON DATABASE diyapp_telemetry TO diyapp_app;
GRANT SELECT, INSERT ON raw_agent_events TO diyapp_app;
GRANT SELECT ON agent_performance_hourly TO diyapp_app;
GRANT SELECT, INSERT ON system_health_metrics TO diyapp_app;

-- User for read-only access (dashboards)
CREATE USER diyapp_reader WITH PASSWORD 'ReaderPassword123!';
GRANT CONNECT ON DATABASE diyapp_telemetry TO diyapp_reader;
GRANT SELECT ON ALL TABLES IN SCHEMA public TO diyapp_reader;
```

### [Sessão Paralela: AI Ops]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core: Sistema de Auto-Otimização de Agentes

Vou implementar um sistema completo de auto-otimização para agentes LLM, incluindo monitoramento de prompts, fine-tuning contínuo e A/B testing de modelos com múltiplos provedores.

```python
# Estrutura do projeto
# diyapp-evolution-v11/

## 1. Configuração Principal

```python
# config/settings.py
import os
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Dict, List, Optional
from datetime import datetime
import json

@dataclass
class ProviderConfig:
    """Configuração para cada provedor LLM"""
    name: str
    api_key: str
    base_url: Optional[str] = None
    default_model: str = "gpt-4"
    cost_per_token: Dict[str, float] = None
    max_tokens: int = 4096
    timeout: int = 30
    
    def __post_init__(self):
        if self.cost_per_token is None:
            self.cost_per_token = {"input": 0.00003, "output": 0.00006}

@dataclass
class OptimizationConfig:
    """Configuração de otimização"""
    evaluation_interval: int = 100  # Avaliar a cada 100 interações
    ab_testing_enabled: bool = True
    fine_tuning_threshold: float = 0.8  # Limiar para iniciar fine-tuning
    max_prompt_length: int = 4000
    min_samples_for_tuning: int = 100
    golden_dataset_path: str = "data/golden_dataset.json"

@dataclass
class MonitoringConfig:
    """Configuração de monitoramento"""
    metrics_retention_days: int = 90
    alert_thresholds: Dict[str, float] = None
    sampling_rate: float = 1.0  # 100% das chamadas são monitoradas
    
    def __post_init__(self):
        if self.alert_thresholds is None:
            self.alert_thresholds = {
                "cost_increase": 0.2,  # 20%
                "quality_decrease": 0.1,  # 10%
                "latency_p95": 8.0,  # 8 segundos
                "error_rate": 0.01,  # 1%
                "fallback_rate": 0.05  # 5%
            }

class Settings:
    """Configurações globais do sistema"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        # Configurações de provedores
        self.providers = {
            "openai": ProviderConfig(
                name="openai",
                api_key=os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY", ""),
                default_model="gpt-4",
                cost_per_token={"input": 0.00003, "output": 0.00006}
            ),
            "anthropic": ProviderConfig(
                name="anthropic",
                api_key=os.getenv("ANTHROPIC_API_KEY", ""),
                default_model="claude-3-sonnet-20240229",
                cost_per_token={"input": 0.000003, "output": 0.000015}
            ),
            "google": ProviderConfig(
                name="google",
                api_key=os.getenv("GOOGLE_API_KEY", ""),
                default_model="gemini-pro",
                cost_per_token={"input": 0.0000005, "output": 0.0000015}
            )
        }
        
        # Configuração de otimização
        self.optimization = OptimizationConfig()
        
        # Configuração de monitoramento
        self.monitoring = MonitoringConfig()
        
        # Configuração do banco de dados
        self.database_url = os.getenv("DATABASE_URL", "sqlite:///diyapp_evolution.db")
        
        # Configuração do servidor
        self.host = os.getenv("HOST", "0.0.0.0")
        self.port = int(os.getenv("PORT", 8080))
        self.debug = os.getenv("DEBUG", "False").lower() == "true"

settings = Settings()
```

## 2. Sistema de Banco de Dados

```python
# src/database/models.py
from sqlalchemy import create_engine, Column, Integer, String, Float, DateTime, Text, JSON, Boolean
from sqlalchemy.ext.declarative import declarative_base
from sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker
import datetime

Base = declarative_base()

class LLMCall(Base):
    """Registro de cada chamada LLM"""
    __tablename__ = "llm_calls"
    
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
    call_id = Column(String(100), unique=True, index=True)
    timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.datetime.utcnow)
    provider = Column(String(50))
    model = Column(String(100))
    feature = Column(String(100))
    input_tokens = Column(Integer)
    output_tokens = Column(Integer)
    cost = Column(Float)
    latency = Column(Float)  # em segundos
    success = Column(Boolean)
    error_message = Column(Text, nullable=True)
    prompt_hash = Column(String(64), index=True)
    response_hash = Column(String(64))
    metadata = Column(JSON)
    fallback_used = Column(Boolean, default=False)
    fallback_reason = Column(String(200), nullable=True)

class PromptTemplate(Base):
    """Templates de prompt otimizados"""
    __tablename__ = "prompt_templates"
    
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
    template_id = Column(String(100), unique=True, index=True)
    feature = Column(String(100))
    template = Column(Text)
    version = Column(Integer, default=1)
    created_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.datetime.utcnow)
    is_active = Column(Boolean, default=True)
    performance_score = Column(Float, default=0.0)
    total_calls = Column(Integer, default=0)
    avg_latency = Column(Float, default=0.0)
    avg_cost = Column(Float, default=0.0)
    metadata = Column(JSON)

class ABTest(Base):
    """Registro de testes A/B"""
    __tablename__ = "ab_tests"
    
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
    test_id = Column(String(100), unique=True, index=True)
    feature = Column(String(100))
    variant_a = Column(String(100))
    variant_b = Column(String(100))
    start_time = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.datetime.utcnow)
    end_time = Column(DateTime, nullable=True)
    total_participants = Column(Integer, default=0)
    variant_a_wins = Column(Integer, default=0)
    variant_b_wins = Column(Integer, default=0)
    confidence_level = Column(Float, default=0.0)
    conclusion = Column(Text, nullable=True)
    metadata = Column(JSON)

class OptimizationSuggestion(Base):
    """Sugestões de otimização geradas automaticamente"""
    __tablename__ = "optimization_suggestions"
    
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
    suggestion_id = Column(String(100), unique=True, index=True)
    timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.datetime.utcnow)
    feature = Column(String(100))
    suggestion_type = Column(String(50))  # 'cost', 'quality', 'latency', 'prompt'
    description = Column(Text)
    current_value = Column(Float)
    expected_improvement = Column(Float)
    confidence = Column(Float)
    implemented = Column(Boolean, default=False)
    implementation_date = Column(DateTime, nullable=True)
    actual_improvement = Column(Float, nullable=True)
    metadata = Column(JSON)

class GoldenDataset(Base):
    """Dataset golden para avaliação de qualidade"""
    __tablename__ = "golden_dataset"
    
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
    dataset_id = Column(String(100), index=True)
    feature = Column(String(100))
    input_text = Column(Text)
    expected_output = Column(Text)
    evaluation_criteria = Column(JSON)
    created_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.datetime.utcnow)
    last_used = Column(DateTime, nullable=True)
    metadata = Column(JSON)

# src/database/connection.py
from sqlalchemy import create_engine
from sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker
from .models import Base
import logging

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class DatabaseManager:
    """Gerenciador de conexão com banco de dados"""
    
    def __init__(self, database_url: str):
        self.engine = create_engine(database_url)
        self.SessionLocal = sessionmaker(autocommit=False, autoflush=False, bind=self.engine)
        
    def init_db(self):
        """Inicializa o banco de dados"""
        try:
            Base.metadata.create_all(bind=self.engine)
            logger.info("Banco de dados inicializado com sucesso")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Erro ao inicializar banco de dados: {e}")
            raise
    
    def get_session(self):
        """Retorna uma sessão do banco de dados"""
        return self.SessionLocal()
    
    def close_session(self, session):
        """Fecha uma sessão do banco de dados"""
        session.close()
```

## 3. Provedores LLM

```python
# src/providers/base.py
from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional, Tuple
import hashlib
import time
import logging
from dataclasses import dataclass

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

@dataclass
class LLMResponse:
    """Resposta padronizada do LLM"""
    content: str
    input_tokens: int
    output_tokens: int
    latency: float
    model: str
    provider: str
    success: bool = True
    error_message: Optional[str] = None
    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = None

class BaseProvider(ABC):
    """Classe base para todos os provedores LLM"""
    
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.name = config.name
        self.api_key = config.api_key
        self.default_model = config.default_model
        self.cost_per_token = config.cost_per_token
        self.timeout = config.timeout
    
    @abstractmethod
    async def generate(self, prompt: str, **kwargs) -> LLMResponse:
        """Gera uma resposta do LLM"""
        pass
    
    def calculate_cost(self, input_tokens: int, output_tokens: int) -> float:
        """Calcula o custo da chamada"""
        input_cost = input_tokens * self.cost_per_token.get("input", 0)
        output_cost = output_tokens * self.cost_per_token.get("output", 0)
        return input_cost + output_cost
    
    def hash_prompt(self, prompt: str) -> str:
        """Gera hash do prompt para tracking"""
        return hashlib.sha256(prompt.encode()).hexdigest()

# src/providers/openai.py
import openai
from .base import BaseProvider, LLMResponse
from typing import Dict, Any

class OpenAIProvider(BaseProvider):
    """Provedor OpenAI"""
    
    def __init__(self, config):
        super().__init__(config)
        openai.api_key = self.api_key
        if config.base_url:
            openai.base_url = config.base_url
    
    async def generate(self, prompt: str, **kwargs) -> LLMResponse:
        """Gera resposta usando OpenAI API"""
        start_time = time.time()
        
        try:
            model = kwargs.get("model", self.default_model)
            max_tokens = kwargs.get("max_tokens", self.config.max_tokens)
            
            response = await openai.ChatCompletion.acreate(
                model=model,
                messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
                max_tokens=max_tokens,
                timeout=self.timeout
            )
            
            latency = time.time() - start_time
            
            return LLMResponse(
                content=response.choices[0].message.content,
                input_tokens=response.usage.prompt_tokens,
                output_tokens=response.usage.completion_tokens,
                latency=latency,
                model=model,
                provider=self.name,
                metadata={
                    "finish_reason": response.choices[0].finish_reason,
                    "response_id": response.id
                }
            )
            
        except Exception as e:
            latency = time.time() - start_time
            logger.error(f"Erro no provedor OpenAI: {e}")
            
            return LLMResponse(
                content="",
                input_tokens=0,
                output_tokens=0,
                latency=latency,
                model=kwargs.get("model", self.default_model),
                provider=self.name,
                success=False,
                error_message=str(e)
            )

# src/providers/anthropic.py
import anthropic
from .base import BaseProvider, LLMResponse

class AnthropicProvider(BaseProvider):
    """Provedor Anthropic"""
    
    def __init__(self, config):
        super().__init__(config)
        self.client = anthropic.AsyncAnthropic(api_key=self.api_key)
    
    async def generate(self, prompt: str, **kwargs) -> LLMResponse:
        """Gera resposta usando Anthropic API"""
        start_time = time.time()
        
        try:
            model = kwargs.get("model", self.default_model)
            max_tokens = kwargs.get("max_tokens", self.config.max_tokens)
            
            response = await self.client.messages.create(
                model=model,
                max_tokens=max_tokens,
                messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}]
            )
            
            latency = time.time() - start_time
            
            return LLMResponse(
                content=response.content[0].text,
                input_tokens=response.usage.input_tokens,
                output_tokens=response.usage.output_tokens,
                latency=latency,
                model=model,
                provider=self.name,
                metadata={
                    "stop_reason": response.stop_reason,
                    "response_id": response.id
                }
            )
            
        except Exception as e:
            latency = time.time() - start_time
            logger.error(f"Erro no provedor Anthropic: {e}")
            
            return LLMResponse(
                content="",
                input_tokens=0,
                output_tokens=0,
                latency=latency,
                model=kwargs.get("model", self.default_model),
                provider=self.name,
                success=False,
                error_message=str(e)
            )

# src/providers/google.py
import google.generativeai as genai
from .base import BaseProvider, LLMResponse

class GoogleProvider(BaseProvider):
    """Provedor Google Gemini"""
    
    def __init__(self, config):
        super().__init__(config)
        genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)
    
    async def generate(self, prompt: str, **kwargs) -> LLMResponse:
        """Gera resposta usando Google Gemini API"""
        start_time = time.time()
        
        try:
            model = kwargs.get("model", self.default_model)
            max_tokens = kwargs.get("max_tokens", self.config.max_tokens)
            
            # Configuração do modelo
            generation_config = {
                "temperature": kwargs.get("temperature", 0.7),
                "top_p": kwargs.get("top_p", 0.95),
                "top_k": kwargs.get("top_k", 40),
                "max_output_tokens": max_tokens,
            }
            
            model_instance = genai.GenerativeModel(
                model_name=model,
                generation_config=generation_config
            )
            
            response = await model_instance.generate_content_async(prompt)
            
            latency = time.time() - start_time
            
            # Estimativa de tokens (Gemini não retorna contagem exata)
            input_tokens = len(prompt.split()) // 0.75  # Estimativa aproximada
            output_tokens = len(response.text.split()) // 0.75
            
            return LLMResponse(
                content=response.text,
                input_tokens=int(input_tokens),
                output_tokens=int(output_tokens),
                latency=latency,
                model=model,
                provider=self.name,
                metadata={
                    "finish_reason": response.candidates[0].finish_reason if response.candidates else None,
                    "safety_ratings": response.prompt_feedback.safety_ratings if response.prompt_feedback else []
                }
            )
            
        except Exception as e:
            latency = time.time() - start_time
            logger.error(f"Erro no provedor Google: {e}")
            
            return LLMResponse(
                content="",
                input_tokens=0,
                output_tokens=0,
                latency=latency,
                model=kwargs.get("model", self.default_model),
                provider=self.name,
                success=False,
                error_message=str(e)
            )
```

resource "aws_cloudwatch_metric_alarm" "availability_slo" {
  alarm_name          = "${var.app_name}-availability-slo-${var.environment}"
  comparison_operator = "LessThanThreshold"
  evaluation_periods  = "5"
  metric_name        = "HealthyHostCount"
  namespace          = "AWS/ApplicationELB"
  period             = "60"
  statistic          = "Average"
  threshold          = var.min_capacity * 0.5  # 50% of min capacity down
  alarm_description  = "Availability SLO violation - less than 50% healthy hosts"
  alarm_actions      = [aws_sns_topic.slo_violations.arn]
  
  dimensions = {
    LoadBalancer = aws_lb.main.arn_suffix
    TargetGroup  = aws_lb_target_group.api.arn_suffix
  }
  
  tags = {
    SLO_Type     = "Availability"
    SLO_Target   = var.slo_availability_target
    Severity     = "Sev1"
  }
}

resource "aws_cloudwatch_metric_alarm" "latency_slo" {
  alarm_name          = "${var.app_name}-latency-slo-${var.environment}"
  comparison_operator = "GreaterThanThreshold"
  evaluation_periods  = "3"
  metric_name        = "TargetResponseTime"
  namespace          = "AWS/ApplicationELB"
  period             = "60"
  statistic          = "p95"
  threshold          = var.slo_latency_target_p95 / 1000.0  # Convert ms to seconds
  alarm_description  = "Latency SLO violation - P95 > ${var.slo_latency_target_p95}ms"
  alarm_actions      = [aws_sns_topic.slo_violations.arn]
  
  dimensions = {
    LoadBalancer = aws_lb.main.arn_suffix
    TargetGroup  = aws_lb_target_group.api.arn_suffix
  }
  
  tags = {
    SLO_Type     = "Latency"
    SLO_Target   = var.slo_latency_target_p95
    Severity     = "Sev2"
  }
}

## 1. Configuração Principal de Segurança

**src/config/security.js**
```javascript
const crypto = require('crypto');

module.exports = {
  // Configurações de Criptografia
  encryption: {
    algorithm: 'aes-256-gcm',
    keyLength: 32,
    ivLength: 16,
    saltRounds: 12,
    
    // Chaves (em produção, usar KMS ou HashiCorp Vault)
    keys: {
      dataEncryption: process.env.DATA_ENCRYPTION_KEY || 
        crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex'),
      tokenEncryption: process.env.TOKEN_ENCRYPTION_KEY || 
        crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex')
    }
  },

  // Configurações de Sessão e Tokens
  session: {
    accessTokenExpiry: '15m',
    refreshTokenExpiry: '7d',
    mfaTokenExpiry: '5m',
    
    // JWT Config
    jwt: {
      algorithm: 'RS256',
      privateKey: process.env.JWT_PRIVATE_KEY,
      publicKey: process.env.JWT_PUBLIC_KEY
    }
  },

  // Rate Limiting
  rateLimit: {
    auth: {
      windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
      max: 5, // 5 tentativas por IP
      message: 'Muitas tentativas de login. Tente novamente mais tarde.'
    },
    api: {
      windowMs: 60 * 1000, // 1 minuto
      max: 100 // 100 requisições por minuto
    }
  },

  // Headers de Segurança
  headers: {
    csp: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:", "https:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
      fontSrc: ["'self'"],
      objectSrc: ["'none'"],
      mediaSrc: ["'self'"],
      frameSrc: ["'none'"]
    },
    hsts: {
      maxAge: 31536000, // 1 ano
      includeSubDomains: true,
      preload: true
    }
  },

  // Validação de Input
  validation: {
    password: {
      minLength: 12,
      requireUppercase: true,
      requireLowercase: true,
      requireNumbers: true,
      requireSpecialChars: true,
      blacklist: ['password', '123456', 'qwerty']
    },
    username: {
      minLength: 3,
      maxLength: 30,
      pattern: /^[a-zA-Z0-9_-]+$/
    }
  },

  // Logging e Auditoria
  audit: {
    logLevel: 'info',
    sensitiveFields: ['password', 'token', 'credit_card', 'ssn'],
    retentionDays: 365
  }
};
```

## 2. Implementação OAuth2.0/OIDC

**src/auth/oauth2.js**
```javascript
const crypto = require('crypto');
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const { URL } = require('url');

class OAuth2Provider {
  constructor(config) {
    this.config = config;
    this.clients = new Map();
    this.authCodes = new Map();
    this.accessTokens = new Map();
    this.refreshTokens = new Map();
  }

  // Registro de Cliente OAuth2
  registerClient(clientInfo) {
    const clientId = crypto.randomBytes(16).toString('hex');
    const clientSecret = crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
    
    const client = {
      id: clientId,
      secret: crypto.createHash('sha256').update(clientSecret).digest('hex'),
      name: clientInfo.name,
      redirectUris: clientInfo.redirectUris,
      scopes: clientInfo.scopes || ['openid', 'profile', 'email'],
      grants: clientInfo.grants || ['authorization_code', 'refresh_token'],
      accessTokenLifetime: 900, // 15 minutos
      refreshTokenLifetime: 604800 // 7 dias
    };

    this.clients.set(clientId, client);
    
    return {
      client_id: clientId,
      client_secret: clientSecret, // Retornado apenas uma vez
      ...client
    };
  }

  // Endpoint de Autorização
  async authorizationEndpoint(req, res) {
    const {
      response_type,
      client_id,
      redirect_uri,
      scope,
      state,
      code_challenge,
      code_challenge_method = 'plain'
    } = req.query;

    // Validações STRIDE
    await this.validateAuthorizationRequest({
      response_type,
      client_id,
      redirect_uri,
      scope,
      state,
      code_challenge,
      code_challenge_method
    });

    // Verifica se usuário está autenticado
    if (!req.session.userId) {
      // Redireciona para login
      req.session.authRequest = {
        client_id,
        redirect_uri,
        scope,
        state,
        code_challenge,
        code_challenge_method
      };
      return res.redirect('/login');
    }

    // Gera código de autorização
    const authCode = this.generateAuthorizationCode({
      userId: req.session.userId,
      clientId: client_id,
      redirectUri: redirect_uri,
      scope,
      codeChallenge: code_challenge,
      codeChallengeMethod: code_challenge_method
    });

    // Redireciona com código
    const redirectUrl = new URL(redirect_uri);
    redirectUrl.searchParams.set('code', authCode);
    if (state) redirectUrl.searchParams.set('state', state);

    res.redirect(redirectUrl.toString());
  }

  // Endpoint de Token
  async tokenEndpoint(req, res) {
    const {
      grant_type,
      code,
      redirect_uri,
      client_id,
      client_secret,
      code_verifier,
      refresh_token
    } = req.body;

    // Validação básica
    if (!grant_type) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        error: 'invalid_request',
        error_description: 'Missing grant_type parameter'
      });
    }

    switch (grant_type) {
      case 'authorization_code':
        return this.handleAuthorizationCodeGrant(req, res);
      case 'refresh_token':
        return this.handleRefreshTokenGrant(req, res);
      case 'client_credentials':
        return this.handleClientCredentialsGrant(req, res);
      default:
        return res.status(400).json({
          error: 'unsupported_grant_type'
        });
    }
  }

  // Grant: Authorization Code
  async handleAuthorizationCodeGrant(req, res) {
    const { code, redirect_uri, client_id, client_secret, code_verifier } = req.body;

    // Valida cliente
    const client = this.clients.get(client_id);
    if (!client) {
      return res.status(401).json({
        error: 'invalid_client',
        error_description: 'Client authentication failed'
      });
    }

    // Valida secret
    const clientSecretHash = crypto.createHash('sha256')
      .update(client_secret)
      .digest('hex');
    
    if (clientSecretHash !== client.secret) {
      return res.status(401).json({
        error: 'invalid_client',
        error_description: 'Client authentication failed'
      });
    }

    // Busca código de autorização
    const authCodeData = this.authCodes.get(code);
    if (!authCodeData) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        error: 'invalid_grant',
        error_description: 'Invalid authorization code'
      });
    }

    // Valida PKCE (Proof Key for Code Exchange)
    if (authCodeData.codeChallenge) {
      if (!code_verifier) {
        return res.status(400).json({
          error: 'invalid_grant',
          error_description: 'Code verifier required'
        });
      }

      const codeChallenge = this.calculateCodeChallenge(
        code_verifier,
        authCodeData.codeChallengeMethod
      );

      if (codeChallenge !== authCodeData.codeChallenge) {
        return res.status(400).json({
          error: 'invalid_grant',
          error_description: 'Invalid code verifier'
        });
      }
    }

    // Valida redirect URI
    if (authCodeData.redirectUri !== redirect_uri) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        error: 'invalid_grant',
        error_description: 'Redirect URI mismatch'
      });
    }

    // Remove código usado (one-time use)
    this.authCodes.delete(code);

    // Gera tokens
    const tokens = await this.generateTokens({
      userId: authCodeData.userId,
      clientId: client_id,
      scope: authCodeData.scope
    });

    res.json({
      access_token: tokens.accessToken,
      token_type: 'Bearer',
      expires_in: client.accessTokenLifetime,
      refresh_token: tokens.refreshToken,
      scope: authCodeData.scope.join(' ')
    });
  }

  // Métodos auxiliares
  generateAuthorizationCode(data) {
    const code = crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
    
    // Expira em 10 minutos
    const expiresAt = Date.now() + (10 * 60 * 1000);
    
    this.authCodes.set(code, {
      ...data,
      expiresAt
    });

    // Limpeza automática de códigos expirados
    setTimeout(() => {
      this.authCodes.delete(code);
    }, 10 * 60 * 1000);

    return code;
  }

  async generateTokens(data) {
    const accessToken = jwt.sign(
      {
        sub: data.userId,
        client_id: data.clientId,
        scope: data.scope,
        token_type: 'access_token'
      },
      this.config.session.jwt.privateKey,
      {
        algorithm: this.config.session.jwt.algorithm,
        expiresIn: this.config.session.accessTokenExpiry,
        issuer: 'diyapp-v11'
      }
    );

    const refreshToken = crypto.randomBytes(64).toString('hex');
    
    // Armazena refresh token com hash
    const refreshTokenHash = crypto.createHash('sha512')
      .update(refreshToken)
      .digest('hex');
    
    this.refreshTokens.set(refreshTokenHash, {
      userId: data.userId,
      clientId: data.clientId,
      scope: data.scope,
      expiresAt: Date.now() + (7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000) // 7 dias
    });

    return { accessToken, refreshToken };
  }

  calculateCodeChallenge(verifier, method) {
    if (method === 'S256') {
      return crypto.createHash('sha256')
        .update(verifier)
        .digest('base64')
        .replace(/\+/g, '-')
        .replace(/\//g, '_')
        .replace(/=/g, '');
    }
    
    // plain
    return verifier;
  }

  async validateAuthorizationRequest(params) {
    // Validações STRIDE implementadas
    const client = this.clients.get(params.client_id);
    
    if (!client) {
      throw new Error('invalid_client');
    }

    // Spoofing: Verifica redirect URI
    if (!client.redirectUris.includes(params.redirect_uri)) {
      throw new Error('invalid_redirect_uri');
    }

    // Tampering: Valida PKCE
    if (params.code_challenge_method && 
        !['plain', 'S256'].includes(params.code_challenge_method)) {
      throw new Error('invalid_code_challenge_method');
    }

    // Info Disclosure: Valida escopos
    const requestedScopes = params.scope ? params.scope.split(' ') : [];
    const invalidScopes = requestedScopes.filter(s => !client.scopes.includes(s));
    
    if (invalidScopes.length > 0) {
      throw new Error('invalid_scope');
    }

    return true;
  }
}

module.exports = OAuth2Provider;
```

**src/auth/oidc.js**
```javascript
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const crypto = require('crypto');

class OIDCProvider extends OAuth2Provider {
  constructor(config) {
    super(config);
    this.userInfo = new Map();
  }

  // Discovery endpoint (/.well-known/openid-configuration)
  getDiscoveryDocument(baseUrl) {
    return {
      issuer: baseUrl,
      authorization_endpoint: `${baseUrl}/oauth/authorize`,
      token_endpoint: `${baseUrl}/oauth/token`,
      userinfo_endpoint: `${baseUrl}/oauth/userinfo`,
      jwks_uri: `${baseUrl}/oauth/jwks`,
      response_types_supported: ['code'],
      subject_types_supported: ['public'],
      id_token_signing_alg_values_supported: ['RS256'],
      scopes_supported: ['openid', 'profile', 'email', 'offline_access'],
      token_endpoint_auth_methods_supported: ['client_secret_basic', 'client_secret_post'],
      claims_supported: ['sub', 'name', 'email', 'email_verified']
    };
  }

  // JWKS endpoint
  getJWKS() {
    // Em produção, gerar par de chaves real
    const publicKey = this.config.session.jwt.publicKey;
    
    // Extrai modulus e exponent da chave pública
    const key = crypto.createPublicKey(publicKey);
    const jwk = key.export({ format: 'jwk' });

    return {
      keys: [{
        kty: jwk.kty,
        use: 'sig',
        kid: 'diyapp-v11-key-1',
        alg: 'RS256',
        n: jwk.n,
        e: jwk.e
      }]
    };
  }

  // UserInfo endpoint
  async getUserInfo(accessToken) {
    try {
      // Decodifica token sem verificar (já foi verificado no middleware)
      const decoded = jwt.decode(accessToken);
      
      if (!decoded || !decoded.sub) {
        throw new Error('invalid_token');
      }

      // Busca informações do usuário
      const userInfo = this.userInfo.get(decoded.sub);
      
      if (!userInfo) {
        throw new Error('user_not_found');
      }

      // Retorna claims OIDC padrão
      return {
        sub: userInfo.id,
        name: userInfo.name,
        given_name: userInfo.givenName,
        family_name: userInfo.familyName,
        email: userInfo.email,
        email_verified: userInfo.emailVerified || false,
        picture: userInfo.picture,
        locale: userInfo.locale || 'pt-BR',
        updated_at: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000)
      };
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error('invalid_token');
    }
  }

  // Gera ID Token (OpenID Connect)
  async generateIdToken(userId, clientId, nonce) {
    const userInfo = this.userInfo.get(userId);
    
    if (!userInfo) {
      throw new Error('user_not_found');
    }

    const idToken = jwt.sign(
      {
        iss: 'diyapp-v11',
        sub: userId,
        aud: clientId,
        exp: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000) + 3600, // 1 hora
        iat: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000),
        auth_time: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000),
        nonce: nonce,
        name: userInfo.name,
        email: userInfo.email,
        email_verified: userInfo.emailVerified || false
      },
      this.config.session.jwt.privateKey,
      {
        algorithm: this.config.session.jwt.algorithm
      }
    );

    return idToken;
  }

  // Registra usuário para OIDC
  registerUser(userData) {
    const userId = `user_${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}`;
    
    this.userInfo.set(userId, {
      id: userId,
      ...userData,
      emailVerified: false
    });

    return userId;
  }

  // Verifica email (simulação)
  verifyEmail(userId) {
    const user = this.userInfo.get(userId);
    
    if (user) {
      user.emailVerified = true;
      this.userInfo.set(userId, user);
      return true;
    }
    
    return false;
  }
}

module.exports = OIDCProvider;
```

    this.createRole('super

**src/compliance/models/DataSubject.js**
```javascript
const { DataTypes } = require('sequelize');
const sequelize = require('../../database/connection');

const DataSubject = sequelize.define('DataSubject', {
  id: {
    type: DataTypes.UUID,
    defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
    primaryKey: true
  },
  externalId: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false,
    unique: true
  },
  email: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false,
    validate: {
      isEmail: true
    }
  },
  name: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: true
  },
  documentNumber: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: true,
    comment: 'CPF ou documento equivalente'
  },
  consentVersion: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false,
    defaultValue: '1.0'
  },
  consentDate: {
    type: DataTypes.DATE,
    allowNull: false,
    defaultValue: DataTypes.NOW
  },
  legalBasis: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM('consent', 'contract', 'legal_obligation', 'legitimate_interest', 'vital_interest', 'public_interest'),
    allowNull: false
  },
  dataCategories: {
    type: DataTypes.JSON,
    allowNull: false,
    defaultValue: []
  },
  retentionPeriod: {
    type: DataTypes.INTEGER,
    allowNull: false,
    defaultValue: 180
  },
  retentionEndDate: {
    type: DataTypes.DATE,
    allowNull: true
  },
  status: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM('active', 'deleted', 'anonymized', 'pending_deletion'),
    defaultValue: 'active'
  },
  deletionRequestDate: {
    type: DataTypes.DATE,
    allowNull: true
  },
  lastAccessDate: {
    type: DataTypes.DATE,
    allowNull: true
  },
  metadata: {
    type: DataTypes.JSON,
    allowNull: true
  }
}, {
  tableName: 'data_subjects',
  timestamps: true,
  paranoid: true,
  indexes: [
    {
      unique: true,
      fields: ['email']
    },
    {
      fields: ['status']
    },
    {
      fields: ['retentionEndDate']
    }
  ]
});

// Hook para calcular data de expiração
DataSubject.beforeSave(async (subject) => {
  if (!subject.retentionEndDate) {
    const retentionDays = subject.retentionPeriod || 180;
    subject.retentionEndDate = new Date();
    subject.retentionEndDate.setDate(subject.retentionEndDate.getDate() + retentionDays);
  }
});

module.exports = DataSubject;

const { DataTypes } = require('sequelize');
const sequelize = require('../../database/connection');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const config = require('../../../config/complianceConfig');

const AuditLog = sequelize.define('AuditLog', {
  id: {
    type: DataTypes.UUID,
    defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
    primaryKey: true
  },
  eventId: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false,
    unique: true
  },
  timestamp: {
    type: DataTypes.DATE,
    allowNull: false,
    defaultValue: DataTypes.NOW
  },
  eventType: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM(
      'data_access',
      'data_modification',
      'data_deletion',
      'consent_change',
      'breach_detection',
      'policy_change',
      'user_request',
      'system_event'
    ),
    allowNull: false
  },
  userId: {
    type: DataTypes.UUID,
    allowNull: true
  },
  userRole: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: true
  },
  dataSubjectId: {
    type: DataTypes.UUID,
    allowNull: true
  },
  ipAddress: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: true
  },
  userAgent: {
    type: DataTypes.TEXT,
    allowNull: true
  },
  resourceType: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false
  },
  resourceId: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: true
  },
  action: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false
  },
  previousValue: {
    type: DataTypes.JSON,
    allowNull: true
  },
  newValue: {
    type: DataTypes.JSON,
    allowNull: true
  },
  changes: {
    type: DataTypes.JSON,
    allowNull: true
  },
  status: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM('success', 'failure', 'warning'),
    defaultValue: 'success'
  },
  errorMessage: {
    type: DataTypes.TEXT,
    allowNull: true
  },
  metadata: {
    type: DataTypes.JSON,
    allowNull: true
  },
  // Campos para imutabilidade
  hash: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false
  },
  previousHash: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: true
  },
  blockchainTxId: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: true
  },
  verified: {
    type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
    defaultValue: false
  }
}, {
  tableName: 'audit_logs',
  timestamps: true,
  indexes: [
    {
      fields: ['timestamp']
    },
    {
      fields: ['eventType']
    },
    {
      fields: ['userId']
    },
    {
      fields: ['dataSubjectId']
    },
    {
      fields: ['hash']
    },
    {
      fields: ['verified']
    }
  ]
});

// Hook para gerar hash imutável
AuditLog.beforeCreate(async (log) => {
  // Gerar ID único do evento
  log.eventId = `audit_${Date.now()}_${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex')}`;
  
  // Calcular hash do registro anterior
  const previousLog = await AuditLog.findOne({
    order: [['timestamp', 'DESC']],
    attributes: ['hash']
  });
  
  if (previousLog) {
    log.previousHash = previousLog.hash;
  }
  
  // Gerar hash atual
  const hashData = JSON.stringify({
    timestamp: log.timestamp,
    eventType: log.eventType,
    userId: log.userId,
    dataSubjectId: log.dataSubjectId,
    action: log.action,
    previousValue: log.previousValue,
    newValue: log.newValue,
    previousHash: log.previousHash
  });
  
  log.hash = crypto
    .createHash(config.audit.hashAlgorithm)
    .update(hashData)
    .digest('hex');
});

// Método para verificar integridade
AuditLog.prototype.verifyIntegrity = async function() {
  const hashData = JSON.stringify({
    timestamp: this.timestamp,
    eventType: this.eventType,
    userId: this.userId,
    dataSubjectId: this.dataSubjectId,
    action: this.action,
    previousValue: this.previousValue,
    newValue: this.newValue,
    previousHash: this.previousHash
  });
  
  const calculatedHash = crypto
    .createHash(config.audit.hashAlgorithm)
    .update(hashData)
    .digest('hex');
  
  return {
    isVerified: this.hash === calculatedHash,
    storedHash: this.hash,
    calculatedHash: calculatedHash,
    timestamp: this.timestamp
  };
};

module.exports = AuditLog;
```

## 3. Serviços de Conformidade

**src/compliance/services/dataSubjectService.js**
```javascript
const DataSubject = require('../models/DataSubject');
const AuditLog = require('../models/AuditLog');
const { Op } = require('sequelize');
const config = require('../../../config/complianceConfig');

class DataSubjectService {
  constructor() {
    this.retentionCheckInterval = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 24 horas
    this.startRetentionMonitor();
  }

  // Registrar novo titular
  async registerDataSubject(data) {
    const auditData = {
      eventType: 'data_access',
      action: 'register_data_subject',
      resourceType: 'DataSubject',
      userId: data.registeredBy
    };

    try {
      const subject = await DataSubject.create({
        externalId: data.externalId,
        email: data.email,
        name: data.name,
        documentNumber: data.documentNumber,
        consentVersion: data.consentVersion || '1.0',
        consentDate: new Date(),
        legalBasis: data.legalBasis,
        dataCategories: data.dataCategories || [],
        retentionPeriod: data.retentionPeriod || config.retention.defaultPeriod,
        metadata: data.metadata || {}
      });

      await AuditLog.create({
        ...auditData,
        dataSubjectId: subject.id,
        newValue: subject.toJSON(),
        status: 'success',
        metadata: { operation: 'create' }
      });

      return subject;
    } catch (error) {
      await AuditLog.create({
        ...auditData,
        status: 'failure',
        errorMessage: error.message,
        metadata: { operation: 'create', error: error.stack }
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  // Processar solicitação de direitos do titular
  async processSubjectRequest(subjectId, requestType, requestData) {
    const subject = await DataSubject.findByPk(subjectId);
    if (!subject) {
      throw new Error('Titular não encontrado');
    }

    const auditData = {
      eventType: 'user_request',
      action: `subject_request_${requestType}`,
      resourceType: 'DataSubject',
      dataSubjectId: subjectId,
      userId: requestData.processedBy
    };

    try {
      let result;
      
      switch (requestType) {
        case 'access':
          result = await this.handleAccessRequest(subject);
          break;
        
        case 'rectification':
          result = await this.handleRectificationRequest(subject, requestData.corrections);
          break;
        
        case 'erasure':
          result = await this.handleErasureRequest(subject);
          break;
        
        case 'portability':
          result = await this.handlePortabilityRequest(subject);
          break;
        
        case 'restriction':
          result = await this.handleRestrictionRequest(subject, requestData.restriction);
          break;
        
        case 'objection':
          result = await this.handleObjectionRequest(subject, requestData.objection);
          break;
        
        default:
          throw new Error('Tipo de solicitação inválido');
      }

      await AuditLog.create({
        ...auditData,
        newValue: result,
        status: 'success',
        metadata: { requestType, requestData }
      });

      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      await AuditLog.create({
        ...auditData,
        status: 'failure',
        errorMessage: error.message,
        metadata: { requestType, requestData, error: error.stack }
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  // Implementação dos direitos específicos
  async handleAccessRequest(subject) {
    return {
      subject: subject.toJSON(),
      dataCategories: subject.dataCategories,
      processingActivities: await this.getSubjectProcessingActivities(subject.id),
      thirdParties: await

### [Sessão Paralela: QA]

## 2. Testes E2E com Cypress

**cypress.config.js**
```javascript
const { defineConfig } = require('cypress');
const grepTags = require('@cypress/grep/src/plugin');

module.exports = defineConfig({
  projectId: 'diyapp-v11',
  viewportWidth: 1920,
  viewportHeight: 1080,
  defaultCommandTimeout: 10000,
  requestTimeout: 15000,
  responseTimeout: 15000,
  pageLoadTimeout: 30000,
  video: true,
  videoCompression: 32,
  screenshotOnRunFailure: true,
  trashAssetsBeforeRuns: true,
  
  env: {
    baseUrl: process.env.BASE_URL || 'http://localhost:3000',
    apiUrl: process.env.API_URL || 'http://localhost:3001',
    grepTags: '',
    grepOmitFiltered: true,
    coverage: process.env.COVERAGE === 'true'
  },
  
  e2e: {
    setupNodeEvents(on, config) {
      require('cypress-mochawesome-reporter/plugin')(on);
      grepTags(on, config);
      
      // Custom tasks for test data
      on('task', {
        generateTestData() {
          return {
            userId: `test-${Date.now()}`,
            email: `test${Date.now()}@diyapp.com`,
            projectName: `Test Project ${Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000)}`
          };
        },
        
        logToFile(message) {
          const fs = require('fs');
          const path = './cypress/logs/test-execution.log';
          const timestamp = new Date().toISOString();
          fs.appendFileSync(path, `[${timestamp}] ${message}\n`);
          return null;
        }
      });
      
      return config;
    },
    specPattern: 'cypress/e2e/**/*.cy.{js,jsx,ts,tsx}',
    supportFile: 'cypress/support/e2e.js',
    experimentalRunAllSpecs: true
  },
  
  reporter: 'cypress-mochawesome-reporter',
  reporterOptions: {
    reportDir: 'reports/cypress',
    charts: true,
    reportPageTitle: 'DIYAPP V11 Test Report',
    embeddedScreenshots: true,
    inlineAssets: true,
    saveAllAttempts: false
  }
});
```

**cypress/support/e2e.js**
```javascript
import './commands';
import '@cypress/grep';
import 'cypress-mochawesome-reporter/register';

// Global before hook
before(() => {
  cy.log('Starting DIYAPP V11 E2E Test Suite');
  
  // Clear test data if needed
  if (Cypress.env('CLEAR_DATA')) {
    cy.request({
      method: 'POST',
      url: `${Cypress.env('apiUrl')}/test/clear-data`,
      failOnStatusCode: false
    });
  }
});

// Global after hook
after(() => {
  cy.log('DIYAPP V11 E2E Test Suite completed');
  
  // Generate coverage report if enabled
  if (Cypress.env('coverage')) {
    cy.task('generateCoverageReport');
  }
});

// Custom error handling
Cypress.on('uncaught:exception', (err, runnable) => {
  // Log the error but don't fail the test
  console.error('Uncaught exception:', err.message);
  
  // Return false to prevent Cypress from failing the test
  // Only for known non-critical errors
  if (err.message.includes('ResizeObserver') || 
      err.message.includes('hydration') ||
      err.message.includes('WebSocket')) {
    return false;
  }
  
  return true;
});
```

**cypress/support/commands.js**
```javascript
// Custom commands for DIYAPP V11

// Authentication commands
Cypress.Commands.add('login', (email = 'admin@diyapp.com', password = 'Test123!') => {
  cy.session([email, password], () => {
    cy.visit('/login');
    cy.get('[data-testid="email-input"]').type(email);
    cy.get('[data-testid="password-input"]').type(password);
    cy.get('[data-testid="login-button"]').click();
    cy.url().should('include', '/dashboard');
    cy.get('[data-testid="user-avatar"]').should('be.visible');
  }, {
    cacheAcrossSpecs: true,
    validate: () => {
      cy.getCookie('session_id').should('exist');
    }
  });
});

Cypress.Commands.add('logout', () => {
  cy.get('[data-testid="user-menu"]').click();
  cy.get('[data-testid="logout-button"]').click();
  cy.url().should('include', '/login');
});

// API commands
Cypress.Commands.add('apiRequest', (method, endpoint, body = null, options = {}) => {
  const defaultOptions = {
    method: method,
    url: `${Cypress.env('apiUrl')}${endpoint}`,
    headers: {
      'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      'Authorization': `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('token')}`
    },
    failOnStatusCode: options.failOnStatusCode !== false
  };
  
  if (body) {
    defaultOptions.body = body;
  }
  
  return cy.request({ ...defaultOptions, ...options });
});

// Database commands
Cypress.Commands.add('seedDatabase', (fixture = 'default') => {
  cy.task('logToFile', `Seeding database with fixture: ${fixture}`);
  return cy.apiRequest('POST', '/test/seed', { fixture });
});

Cypress.Commands.add('cleanDatabase', () => {
  cy.task('logToFile', 'Cleaning test database');
  return cy.apiRequest('POST', '/test/clean');
});

// Performance monitoring
Cypress.Commands.add('measurePerformance', (metricName, threshold = 2000) => {
  const startTime = performance.now();
  
  return {
    stop: () => {
      const endTime = performance.now();
      const duration = endTime - startTime;
      
      cy.task('logToFile', `Performance metric [${metricName}]: ${duration}ms`);
      
      if (duration > threshold) {
        cy.log(`⚠️ Performance warning: ${metricName} took ${duration}ms (threshold: ${threshold}ms)`);
      }
      
      return duration;
    }
  };
});

// Error scenario helpers
Cypress.Commands.add('simulateNetworkError', () => {
  cy.intercept('**', { forceNetworkError: true }).as('networkError');
});

Cypress.Commands.add('simulateSlowResponse', (delay = 5000) => {
  cy.intercept('**', (req) => {
    req.on('response', (res) => {
      res.setDelay(delay);
    });
  }).as('slowResponse');
});

// Accessibility testing
Cypress.Commands.add('checkAccessibility', () => {
  cy.injectAxe();
  cy.checkA11y(null, {
    includedImpacts: ['critical', 'serious'],
    rules: {
      'color-contrast': { enabled: false } // Disable if design system is validated
    }
  });
});

// Screenshot comparison
Cypress.Commands.add('compareScreenshot', (name, options = {}) => {
  const threshold = options.threshold || 0.1;
  
  cy.screenshot(name, options);
  cy.task('compareScreenshots', {
    name,
    threshold,
    specName: Cypress.spec.name
  }).then((result) => {
    if (result.mismatch > threshold) {
      throw new Error(`Visual regression detected: ${result.mismatch}% mismatch`);
    }
  });
});
```

## 3. Testes E2E - Fluxos Críticos

**cypress/e2e/critical-flows/authentication.cy.js**
```javascript
describe('DIYAPP V11 - Authentication Critical Flows', { tags: ['critical', 'auth'] }, () => {
  beforeEach(() => {
    cy.cleanDatabase();
    cy.visit('/');
  });

  it('should successfully login with valid credentials', () => {
    cy.login('admin@diyapp.com', 'Test123!');
    
    cy.url().should('include', '/dashboard');
    cy.get('[data-testid="welcome-message"]')
      .should('contain.text', 'Welcome, Admin');
    
    // Verify session persistence
    cy.reload();
    cy.url().should('include', '/dashboard');
  });

  it('should show error with invalid credentials', () => {
    cy.visit('/login');
    cy.get('[data-testid="email-input"]').type('invalid@email.com');
    cy.get('[data-testid="password-input"]').type('wrongpassword');
    cy.get('[data-testid="login-button"]').click();
    
    cy.get('[data-testid="error-message"]')
      .should('be.visible')
      .and('contain.text', 'Invalid credentials');
    
    // Should remain on login page
    cy.url().should('include', '/login');
  });

  it('should handle password reset flow', () => {
    cy.visit('/forgot-password');
    cy.get('[data-testid="email-input"]').type('admin@diyapp.com');
    cy.get('[data-testid="reset-button"]').click();
    
    cy.get('[data-testid="success-message"]')
      .should('be.visible')
      .and('contain.text', 'Reset email sent');
    
    // Verify email was sent (mock)
    cy.apiRequest('GET', '/test/emails')
      .then((response) => {
        expect(response.body).to.have.length.at.least(1);
        expect(response.body[0].to).to.equal('admin@diyapp.com');
        expect(response.body[0].subject).to.include('Password Reset');
      });
  });

  it('should logout successfully', () => {
    cy.login();
    cy.logout();
    
    cy.url().should('include', '/login');
    cy.getCookie('session_id').should('not.exist');
  });

  it('should prevent access to protected routes without authentication', () => {
    const protectedRoutes = ['/dashboard', '/projects', '/settings'];
    
    protectedRoutes.forEach((route) => {
      cy.visit(route);
      cy.url().should('include', '/login');
      cy.get('[data-testid="login-form"]').should('be.visible');
    });
  });

  it('should handle session timeout', () => {
    cy.login();
    
    // Mock session expiration
    cy.apiRequest('POST', '/test/expire-session');
    
    // Try to access protected route
    cy.visit('/dashboard');
    
    // Should redirect to login
    cy.url().should('include', '/login');
    cy.get('[data-testid="session-expired-message"]')
      .should('be.visible');
  });

  it('should maintain session across tabs', () => {
    cy.login();
    
    // Open new tab
    cy.window().then((win) => {
      win.open('/', '_blank');
    });
    
    // Switch to new tab
    cy.window().then((win) => {
      const newWindow = win.open('/', '_blank');
      cy.wrap(newWindow).its('location.href').should('include', '/dashboard');
    });
  });
});
```

describe('DIYAPP V11 - Project Management Critical Flows', { tags: ['critical', 'projects'] }, () => {

      name: 'Concurrent Project',
      description: 'Created by API'

    cy.get('[data-testid="create-project-button"]').click();

      .should('be.visible');

    // Try to submit empty form
    cy.get('[data-testid="create-project-button"]').click();

      .should('be.visible')
      .and('contain.text', 'Name is required

## 2. .env.example

# Server
NODE_ENV=production
PORT=3000
API_KEY=your-secure-api-key

# Database
DB_PATH=./data/optimization.db
DB_BACKUP_PATH=./backups

# LLM Providers
OPENAI_API_KEY=sk-your-openai-key
ANTHROPIC_API_KEY=your-anthropic-key
GOOGLE_API_KEY=your-google-key

# Monitoring
LANGSMITH_API_KEY=your-langsmith-key
HELICONE_API_KEY=your-helicone-key
METRICS_RETENTION_DAYS=90

# Optimization
OPTIMIZATION_THRESHOLD=0.1  # 10% degradation threshold
MIN_SAMPLES_FOR_TUNING=1000
A_B_TEST_DURATION_DAYS=7
COST_ALERT_THRESHOLD=0.2    # 20% cost increase
QUALITY_ALERT_THRESHOLD=0.1 # 10% quality drop

# Fallback Strategy
PRIMARY_PROVIDER=openai
SECONDARY_PROVIDER=anthropic
FALLBACK_TIMEOUT_MS=8000
MAX_RETRIES=3
```
