## 4. src/core/agent-optimizer.js

```javascript
const winston = require('winston');
const cron = require('node-cron');
const { Op } = require('sequelize');

class AgentOptimizer {
    constructor(config = {}) {
        this.config = {
            optimizationThreshold: config.optimizationThreshold || 0.1,
            minSamplesForTuning: config.minSamplesForTuning || 1000,
            abTestDurationDays: config.abTestDurationDays || 7,
            costAlertThreshold: config.costAlertThreshold || 0.2,
            qualityAlertThreshold: config.qualityAlertThreshold || 0.1,
            ...config
        };

        this.logger = winston.createLogger({
            level: 'info',
            format: winston.format.combine(
                winston.format.timestamp(),
                winston.format.json()
            ),
            transports: [
                new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/optimization.log' }),
                new winston.transports.Console()
            ]
        });

        this.metricsCollector = null;
        this.llmGateway = null;
        this.db = null;
        
        this.optimizationHistory = [];
        this.activeExperiments = new Map();
    }

    async initialize({ metricsCollector, llmGateway, db }) {
        this.metricsCollector = metricsCollector;
        this.llmGateway = llmGateway;
        this.db = db;

        // Schedule optimization tasks
        this.scheduleOptimizationTasks();

        this.logger.info('AgentOptimizer initialized');
        return this;
    }

    scheduleOptimizationTasks() {
        // Daily optimization check at 2 AM
        cron.schedule('0 2 * * *', () => this.dailyOptimizationCheck());

        // Hourly metrics analysis
        cron.schedule('0 * * * *', () => this.hourlyMetricsAnalysis());

        // Weekly report generation (Monday 9 AM)
        cron.schedule('0 9 * * 1', () => this.generateWeeklyReport());

        // Continuous A/B test monitoring
        cron.schedule('*/15 * * * *', () => this.monitorActiveExperiments());

        this.logger.info('Optimization tasks scheduled');
    }

    async dailyOptimizationCheck() {
        try {
            this.logger.info('Starting daily optimization check');

            // 1. Collect metrics from last 24 hours
            const metrics = await this.metricsCollector.getDailyMetrics();
            
            // 2. Check for quality degradation
            const qualityIssues = await this.detectQualityDegradation(metrics);
            
            // 3. Check for cost anomalies
            const costIssues = await this.detectCostAnomalies(metrics);
            
            // 4. Check for performance issues
            const performanceIssues = await this.detectPerformanceIssues(metrics);
            
            // 5. Generate optimization suggestions
            const suggestions = await this.generateOptimizationSuggestions({
                qualityIssues,
                costIssues,
                performanceIssues,
                metrics
            });

            // 6. Apply automatic optimizations (if any)
            const appliedOptimizations = await this.applyAutomaticOptimizations(suggestions);

            // 7. Log results
            await this.logOptimizationResults({
                timestamp: new Date(),
                metrics,
                qualityIssues,
                costIssues,
                performanceIssues,
                suggestions,
                appliedOptimizations
            });

            this.logger.info('Daily optimization check completed', {
                qualityIssues: qualityIssues.length,
                costIssues: costIssues.length,
                performanceIssues: performanceIssues.length,
                suggestions: suggestions.length,
                appliedOptimizations: appliedOptimizations.length
            });

            return {
                success: true,
                results: {
                    qualityIssues,
                    costIssues,
                    performanceIssues,
                    suggestions,
                    appliedOptimizations
                }
            };

        } catch (error) {
            this.logger.error('Error in daily optimization check', { error: error.message });
            return { success: false, error: error.message };
        }
    }

    async detectQualityDegradation(metrics) {
        const issues = [];
        
        // Get golden dataset results

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
```hcl
# ============================================
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core
# Infrastructure as Code - Multi-Cloud Setup
# SRE Senior: Multi-Cloud Terraform + Observability
# ============================================

# ============================================
# 1. PROVIDERS CONFIGURATION (Multi-Cloud)
# ============================================

terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.5.0"
  
  required_providers {
    # AWS Provider
    aws = {
      source  = "hashicorp/aws"
      version = "~> 5.0"
    }
    
    # Google Cloud Provider
    google = {
      source  = "hashicorp/google"
      version = "~> 5.0"
    }
    
    # Azure Provider
    azurerm = {
      source  = "hashicorp/azurerm"
      version = "~> 3.0"
    }
    
    # Grafana Provider
    grafana = {
      source  = "grafana/grafana"
      version = "~> 2.0"
    }
    
    # Prometheus Provider
    prometheus = {
      source  = "prometheus-community/prometheus"
      version = "~> 0.20"
    }
  }
  
  backend "s3" {
    bucket         = "diyapp-v11-tfstate"
    key            = "multi-cloud/terraform.tfstate"
    region         = "us-east-1"
    encrypt        = true
    dynamodb_table = "diyapp-tf-locks"
  }
}

# AWS Provider Configuration
provider "aws" {
  region = var.aws_region
  
  default_tags {
    tags = {
      Project     = "DIYAPP-V11"
      Environment = var.environment
      ManagedBy   = "Terraform"
      Squad       = "Autonomous-SRE"
    }
  }
}

# Google Cloud Provider Configuration
provider "google" {
  project = var.gcp_project_id
  region  = var.gcp_region
}

# Azure Provider Configuration
provider "azurerm" {
  features {}
  subscription_id = var.azure_subscription_id
  tenant_id       = var.azure_tenant_id
}

# ============================================
# 2. VARIABLES DEFINITION
# ============================================

variable "environment" {
  description = "Environment (staging/production)"
  type        = string
  default     = "staging"
  
  validation {
    condition     = contains(["staging", "production"], var.environment)
    error_message = "Environment must be 'staging' or 'production'."
  }
}

variable "aws_region" {
  description = "AWS region"
  type        = string
  default     = "us-east-1"
}

variable "gcp_region" {
  description = "GCP region"
  type        = string
  default     = "us-central1"
}

variable "azure_region" {
  description = "Azure region"
  type        = string
  default     = "East US"
}

variable "gcp_project_id" {
  description = "GCP Project ID"
  type        = string
  sensitive   = true
}

variable "azure_subscription_id" {
  description = "Azure Subscription ID"
  type        = string
  sensitive   = true
}

variable "azure_tenant_id" {
  description = "Azure Tenant ID"
  type        = string
  sensitive   = true
}

variable "app_version" {
  description = "Application version"
  type        = string
  default     = "v11.0.0"
}

variable "slo_availability_target" {
  description = "SLO Availability Target (e.g., 0.9995 for 99.95%)"
  type        = number
  default     = 0.9995
}

variable "slo_latency_target_ms" {
  description = "SLO Latency Target in milliseconds (P95)"
  type        = number
  default     = 300
}

variable "slo_error_rate_target" {
  description = "SLO Error Rate Target (e.g., 0.001 for 0.1%)"
  type        = number
  default     = 0.001
}

# ============================================
# 3. STAGING ENVIRONMENT MODULE
# ============================================

module "staging_environment" {
  source = "./modules/environment"
  
  count = var.environment == "staging" ? 1 : 0
  
  environment          = "staging"
  app_version          = var.app_version
  aws_region           = var.aws_region
  gcp_region           = var.gcp_region
  azure_region         = var.azure_region
  gcp_project_id       = var.gcp_project_id
  azure_subscription_id = var.azure_subscription_id
  
  # Auto-scaling configuration for staging
  min_capacity     = 2
  max_capacity     = 4
  target_cpu_util  = 60
  target_mem_util  = 70
  
  # SLO Configuration
  slo_availability_target = var.slo_availability_target
  slo_latency_target_ms   = var.slo_latency_target_ms
  slo_error_rate_target   = var.slo_error_rate_target
}

# ============================================
# 4. PRODUCTION ENVIRONMENT MODULE
# ============================================

module "production_environment" {
  source = "./modules/environment"
  
  count = var.environment == "production" ? 1 : 0
  
  environment          = "production"
  app_version          = var.app_version
  aws_region           = var.aws_region
  gcp_region           = var.gcp_region
  azure_region         = var.azure_region
  gcp_project_id       = var.gcp_project_id
  azure_subscription_id = var.azure_subscription_id
  
  # Auto-scaling configuration for production
  min_capacity     = 4
  max_capacity     = 20
  target_cpu_util  = 70
  target_mem_util  = 75
  
  # SLO Configuration
  slo_availability_target = var.slo_availability_target
  slo_latency_target_ms   = var.slo_latency_target_ms
  slo_error_rate_target   = var.slo_error_rate_target
}

# ============================================
# 5. OBSERVABILITY STACK
# ============================================

module "observability" {
  source = "./modules/observability"
  
  environment = var.environment
  app_version = var.app_version
  
  # SLO Targets
  availability_slo_target = var.slo_availability_target
  latency_slo_target_ms   = var.slo_latency_target_ms
  error_rate_slo_target   = var.slo_error_rate_target
  
  # Cloud-specific configurations
  aws_account_id   = module.staging_environment[0].aws_account_id
  gcp_project_id   = var.gcp_project_id
  azure_resource_group = module.staging_environment[0].azure_resource_group_name
  
  depends_on = [
    module.staging_environment,
    module.production_environment
  ]
}

# ============================================
# 6. OUTPUTS
# ============================================

output "environment_urls" {
  description = "Access URLs for the deployed environment"
  value = var.environment == "staging" ? {
    aws_load_balancer   = module.staging_environment[0].aws_load_balancer_dns
    gcp_load_balancer   = module.staging_environment[0].gcp_load_balancer_ip
    azure_load_balancer = module.staging_environment[0].azure_load_balancer_ip
    grafana_dashboard   = module.observability.grafana_dashboard_url
    prometheus_endpoint = module.observability.prometheus_endpoint
  } : {
    aws_load_balancer   = module.production_environment[0].aws_load_balancer_dns
    gcp_load_balancer   = module.production_environment[0].gcp_load_balancer_ip
    azure_load_balancer = module.production_environment[0].azure_load_balancer_ip
    grafana_dashboard   = module.observability.grafana_dashboard_url
    prometheus_endpoint = module.observability.prometheus_endpoint
  }
}

output "slo_configuration" {
  description = "SLO Configuration Summary"
  value = {
    availability_target = "${var.slo_availability_target * 100}%"
    latency_target      = "${var.slo_latency_target_ms}ms (P95)"
    error_rate_target   = "${var.slo_error_rate_target * 100}%"
    monthly_error_budget_minutes = ceil((1 - var.slo_availability_target) * 30 * 24 * 60)
  }
}

output "provisioning_time" {
  description = "Estimated provisioning time"
  value = "Staging environment provisioned in ~5 minutes"
}

# ============================================
# MODULES/environment/main.tf
# ============================================

# File: modules/environment/main.tf

# AWS Resources
resource "aws_vpc" "main" {
  cidr_block = "10.0.0.0/16"
  
  tags = {
    Name = "diyapp-${var.environment}-vpc"
  }
}

resource "aws_subnet" "public" {
  count             = 2
  vpc_id            = aws_vpc.main.id
  cidr_block        = "10.0.${count.index}.0/24"
  availability_zone = "${var.aws_region}${count.index == 0 ? "a" : "b"}"
  
  tags = {
    Name = "diyapp-${var.environment}-public-${count.index}"
  }
}

resource "aws_ecs_cluster" "main" {
  name = "diyapp-${var.environment}-cluster"
  
  setting {
    name  = "containerInsights"
    value = "enabled"
  }
}

resource "aws_ecs_task_definition" "app" {
  family                   = "diyapp-${var.environment}-task"
  network_mode             = "awsvpc"
  requires_compatibilities = ["FARGATE"]
  cpu                      = 1024
  memory                   = 2048
  
  container_definitions = jsonencode([
    {
      name      = "diyapp-v11"
      image     = "diyapp/v11:${var.app_version}"
      cpu       = 1024
      memory    = 2048
      essential = true
      portMappings = [
        {
          containerPort = 8080
          hostPort      = 8080
          protocol      = "tcp"
        }
      ]
      environment = [
        {
          name  = "ENVIRONMENT"
          value = var.environment
        },
        {
          name  = "APP_VERSION"
          value = var.app_version
        }
      ]
      logConfiguration = {
        logDriver = "awslogs"
        options = {
          "awslogs-group"         = "/ecs/diyapp-${var.environment}"
          "awslogs-region"        = var.aws_region
          "awslogs-stream-prefix" = "ecs"
        }
      }
    }
  ])
}

resource "aws_ecs_service" "main" {
  name            = "diyapp-${var.environment}-service"
  cluster         = aws_ecs_cluster.main.id
  task_definition = aws_ecs_task_definition.app.arn
  desired_count   = var.min_capacity
  launch_type     = "FARGATE"
  
  network_configuration {
    subnets          = aws_subnet.public[*].id
    security_groups  = [aws_security_group.ecs.id]
    assign_public_ip = true
  }
  
  load_balancer {
    target_group_arn = aws_lb_target_group.main.arn
    container_name   = "diyapp-v11"
    container_port   = 8080
  }
  
  # Auto-scaling configuration
  capacity_provider_strategy {
    capacity_provider = "FARGATE"
    weight            = 1
    base              = var.min_capacity
  }
}

# Auto-scaling Policy
resource "aws_appautoscaling_target" "ecs_target" {
  max_capacity       = var.max_capacity
  min_capacity       = var.min_capacity
  resource_id        = "service/${aws_ecs_cluster.main.name}/${aws_ecs_service.main.name}"
  scalable_dimension = "ecs:service:DesiredCount"
  service_namespace  = "ecs"
}

resource "aws_appautoscaling_policy" "cpu_scaling" {
  name               = "cpu-scaling-policy"
  policy_type        = "TargetTrackingScaling"
  resource_id        = aws_appautoscaling_target.ecs_target.resource_id
  scalable_dimension = aws_appautoscaling_target.ecs_target.scalable_dimension
  service_namespace  = aws_appautoscaling_target.ecs_target.service_namespace
  
  target_tracking_scaling_policy_configuration {
    predefined_metric_specification {
      predefined_metric_type = "ECSServiceAverageCPUUtilization"
    }
    target_value       = var.target_cpu_util
    scale_in_cooldown  = 300
    scale_out_cooldown = 60
  }
}

resource "aws_appautoscaling_policy" "memory_scaling" {
  name               = "memory-scaling-policy"
  policy_type        = "TargetTrackingScaling"
  resource_id        = aws_appautoscaling_target.ecs_target.resource_id
  scalable_dimension = aws_appautoscaling_target.ecs_target.scalable_dimension
  service_namespace  = aws_appautoscaling_target.ecs_target.service_namespace
  
  target_tracking_scaling_policy_configuration {
    predefined_metric_specification {
      predefined_metric_type = "ECSServiceAverageMemoryUtilization"
    }
    target_value       = var.target_mem_util
    scale_in_cooldown  = 300
    scale_out_cooldown = 60
  }
}

# Load Balancer
resource "aws_lb" "main" {
  name               = "diyapp-${var.environment}-lb"
  internal           = false
  load_balancer_type = "application"
  security_groups    = [aws_security_group.lb.id]
  subnets            = aws_subnet.public[*].id
  
  enable_deletion_protection = var.environment == "production"
}

resource "aws_lb_listener" "main" {
  load_balancer_arn = aws_lb.main.arn
  port              = "80"
  protocol          = "HTTP"
  
  default_action {
    type             = "forward"
    target_group_arn = aws_lb_target_group.main.arn
  }
}

## 2. Implementação OAuth2.0/OIDC (src/auth/oauth2.js)

```javascript
const passport = require('passport');
const OAuth2Strategy = require('passport-oauth2').Strategy;
const OpenIDConnectStrategy = require('passport-openidconnect').Strategy;
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const crypto = require('crypto');

class OAuth2Security {
  constructor() {
    this.clients = new Map();
    this.authCodes = new Map();
    this.accessTokens = new Map();
    this.refreshTokens = new Map();
    this.init();
  }

  init() {
    // Configuração OAuth2
    passport.use('oauth2', new OAuth2Strategy({
      authorizationURL: process.env.OAUTH2_AUTH_URL || 'https://auth.diyapp.com/oauth/authorize',
      tokenURL: process.env.OAUTH2_TOKEN_URL || 'https://auth.diyapp.com/oauth/token',
      clientID: process.env.OAUTH2_CLIENT_ID,
      clientSecret: process.env.OAUTH2_CLIENT_SECRET,
      callbackURL: process.env.OAUTH2_CALLBACK_URL || 'https://app.diyapp.com/auth/callback',
      state: true,
      scope: ['openid', 'profile', 'email']
    },
    (accessToken, refreshToken, profile, done) => {
      this.verifyOAuth2User(accessToken, refreshToken, profile, done);
    }));

    // Configuração OIDC
    passport.use('oidc', new OpenIDConnectStrategy({
      issuer: process.env.OIDC_ISSUER || 'https://auth.diyapp.com',
      authorizationURL: process.env.OIDC_AUTH_URL || 'https://auth.diyapp.com/oidc/authorize',
      tokenURL: process.env.OIDC_TOKEN_URL || 'https://auth.diyapp.com/oidc/token',
      userInfoURL: process.env.OIDC_USERINFO_URL || 'https://auth.diyapp.com/oidc/userinfo',
      clientID: process.env.OIDC_CLIENT_ID,
      clientSecret: process.env.OIDC_CLIENT_SECRET,
      callbackURL: process.env.OIDC_CALLBACK_URL || 'https://app.diyapp.com/oidc/callback',
      scope: ['openid', 'profile', 'email', 'offline_access']
    },
    (issuer, profile, done) => {
      this.verifyOIDCUser(issuer, profile, done);
    }));

    // Serialização do usuário
    passport.serializeUser((user, done) => {
      done(null, user.id);
    });

    passport.deserializeUser(async (id, done) => {
      try {
        const user = await this.getUserById(id);
        done(null, user);
      } catch (error) {
        done(error);
      }
    });
  }

  async verifyOAuth2User(accessToken, refreshToken, profile, done) {
    try {
      // Validação do token
      const isValid = await this.validateAccessToken(accessToken);
      if (!isValid) {
        return done(new Error('Invalid access token'), null);
      }

      // Busca ou cria usuário
      let user = await this.findUserByProfile(profile);
      if (!user) {
        user = await this.createUserFromProfile(profile);
      }

      // Atualiza tokens
      await this.storeTokens(user.id, accessToken, refreshToken);

      return done(null, user);
    } catch (error) {
      return done(error, null);
    }
  }

  async verifyOIDCUser(issuer, profile, done) {
    try {
      // Validação do issuer
      if (issuer !== process.env.OIDC_ISSUER) {
        return done(new Error('Invalid issuer'), null);
      }

      // Validação do ID Token
      const idToken = profile.id_token;
      const decoded = await this.validateIdToken(idToken);
      
      if (!decoded) {
        return done(new Error('Invalid ID token'), null);
      }

      // Busca ou cria usuário
      let user = await this.findUserByOIDCProfile(profile);
      if (!user) {
        user = await this.createUserFromOIDCProfile(profile);
      }

      // Verifica se o email foi verificado
      if (profile._json.email_verified !== true) {
        return done(new Error('Email not verified'), null);
      }

      return done(null, user);
    } catch (error) {
      return done(error, null);
    }
  }

  async validateAccessToken(token) {
    try {
      // Verifica se o token está na lista de revogados
      if (this.accessTokens.has(token)) {
        const tokenData = this.accessTokens.get(token);
        if (tokenData.revoked || Date.now() > tokenData.expires) {
          return false;
        }
      }

      // Validação JWT
      const decoded = jwt.verify(token, process.env.JWT_SECRET, {
        algorithms: ['RS256', 'HS256'],
        issuer: process.env.JWT_ISSUER
      });

      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  async validateIdToken(token) {
    try {
      const decoded = jwt.verify(token, process.env.OIDC_PUBLIC_KEY, {
        algorithms: ['RS256'],
        issuer: process.env.OIDC_ISSUER,
        audience: process.env.OIDC_CLIENT_ID
      });

      // Verifica nonce para prevenir replay attacks
      if (!decoded.nonce) {
        throw new Error('Missing nonce in ID token');
      }

      // Verifica tempo de expiração
      const now = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
      if (decoded.exp < now) {
        throw new Error('ID token expired');
      }

      return decoded;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('ID token validation failed:', error);
      return null;
    }
  }

  async generateAuthCode(clientId, userId, scope, redirectUri) {
    const code = crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
    const expires = Date.now() + (10 * 60 * 1000); // 10 minutos
    
    this.authCodes.set(code, {
      clientId,
      userId,
      scope,
      redirectUri,
      expires,
      used: false
    });

    // Limpeza automática de códigos expirados
    setTimeout(() => {
      this.authCodes.delete(code);
    }, 10 * 60 * 1000);

    return code;
  }

  async exchangeCodeForToken(code, clientId, clientSecret) {
    const authCode = this.authCodes.get(code);
    
    if (!authCode) {
      throw new Error('Invalid authorization code');
    }

    if (authCode.used) {
      throw new Error('Authorization code already used');
    }

    if (Date.now() > authCode.expires) {
      throw new Error('Authorization code expired');
    }

    if (authCode.clientId !== clientId) {
      throw new Error('Client ID mismatch');
    }

    // Valida client secret
    const client = this.clients.get(clientId);
    if (!client || client.secret !== clientSecret) {
      throw new Error('Invalid client credentials');
    }

    // Marca código como usado
    authCode.used = true;

    // Gera tokens
    const accessToken = this.generateAccessToken(authCode.userId, authCode.scope);
    const refreshToken = this.generateRefreshToken(authCode.userId);

    return {
      access_token: accessToken,
      refresh_token: refreshToken,
      token_type: 'Bearer',
      expires_in: 3600,
      scope: authCode.scope.join(' ')
    };
  }

  generateAccessToken(userId, scope) {
    const token = jwt.sign(
      {
        sub: userId,
        scope: scope,
        iat: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000),
        exp: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000) + 3600 // 1 hora
      },
      process.env.JWT_SECRET,
      { algorithm: 'RS256' }
    );

    this.accessTokens.set(token, {
      userId,
      scope,
      issued: Date.now(),
      expires: Date.now() + (3600 * 1000),
      revoked: false
    });

    return token;
  }

  generateRefreshToken(userId) {
    const token = crypto.randomBytes(64).toString('hex');
    
    this.refreshTokens.set(token, {
      userId,
      issued: Date.now(),
      expires: Date.now() + (30 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000), // 30 dias
      revoked: false
    });

    return token;
  }

  async refreshAccessToken(refreshToken) {
    const tokenData = this.refreshTokens.get(refreshToken);
    
    if (!tokenData) {
      throw new Error('Invalid refresh token');
    }

    if (tokenData.revoked) {
      throw new Error('Refresh token revoked');
    }

    if (Date.now() > tokenData.expires) {
      throw new Error('Refresh token expired');
    }

    // Gera novo access token
    const user = await this.getUserById(tokenData.userId);
    const accessToken = this.generateAccessToken(user.id, user.scope);

    return {
      access_token: accessToken,
      token_type: 'Bearer',
      expires_in: 3600
    };
  }

  async revokeToken(token, tokenType = 'access_token') {
    if (tokenType === 'access_token') {
      if (this.accessTokens.has(token)) {
        this.accessTokens.get(token).revoked = true;
      }
    } else if (tokenType === 'refresh_token') {
      if (this.refreshTokens.has(token)) {
        this.refreshTokens.get(token).revoked = true;
      }
    }
  }

  // Métodos auxiliares (implementação real dependeria do banco de dados)
  async getUserById(id) {
    // Implementação real buscaria do banco de dados
    return { id, email: 'user@example.com', scope: ['read', 'write'] };
  }

  async findUserByProfile(profile) {
    // Implementação real
    return null;
  }

  async createUserFromProfile(profile) {
    // Implementação real
    return { id: crypto.randomUUID(), ...profile };
  }

  async findUserByOIDCProfile(profile) {
    // Implementação real
    return null;
  }

  async createUserFromOIDCProfile(profile) {
    // Implementação real
    return { id: crypto.randomUUID(), ...profile };
  }

  async storeTokens(userId, accessToken, refreshToken) {
    // Implementação real armazenaria no banco de dados
    console.log(`Tokens stored for user ${userId}`);
  }
}

module.exports = OAuth2Security;
```

## 3. Implementação RBAC Granular (src/auth/rbac.js)

```javascript
const { Sequelize, DataTypes } = require('sequelize');

class RBACSystem {
  constructor() {
    this.sequelize = new Sequelize({
      dialect: 'sqlite',
      storage: './database/rbac.sqlite',
      logging: false
    });

    this.initModels();
    this.initDefaultRoles();
  }

  async initModels() {
    // Modelo de Usuário
    this.User = this.sequelize.define('User', {
      id: {
        type: DataTypes.UUID,
        defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
        primaryKey: true
      },
      email: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING,
        unique: true,
        allowNull: false,
        validate: {
          isEmail: true
        }
      },
      isActive: {
        type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
        defaultValue: true
      },
      mfaEnabled: {
        type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
        defaultValue: false
      },
      lastLogin: {
        type: DataTypes.DATE
      }
    });

    // Modelo de Role
    this.Role = this.sequelize.define('Role', {
      id: {
        type: DataTypes.UUID,
        defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
        primaryKey: true
      },
      name: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING,
        unique: true,
        allowNull: false
      },
      description: {
        type: DataTypes.TEXT
      },
      level: {
        type: DataTypes.INTEGER,
        defaultValue: 0
      }
    });

    // Modelo de Permissão
    this.Permission = this.sequelize.define('Permission', {
      id: {
        type: DataTypes.UUID,
        defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
        primaryKey: true
      },
      resource: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING,
        allowNull: false
      },
      action: {
        type: DataTypes.ENUM('create', 'read', 'update', 'delete', 'execute'),
        allowNull: false
      },
      conditions: {
        type: DataTypes.JSON,
        defaultValue: {}
      }
    });

    // Modelo de Session
    this.Session = this.sequelize.define('Session', {
      id: {
        type: DataTypes.UUID,
        defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
        primaryKey: true
      },
      userId: {
        type: DataTypes.UUID,
        allowNull: false
      },
      token: {
        type: DataTypes.TEXT,
        allowNull: false
      },
      ipAddress: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING
      },
      userAgent: {
        type: DataTypes.TEXT
      },
      expiresAt: {
        type: DataTypes.DATE,
        allowNull: false
      },
      revoked: {
        type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
        defaultValue: false
      }
    });

    // Relacionamentos
    this.User.belongsToMany(this.Role, { through: 'UserRoles' });
    this.Role.belongsToMany(this.User, { through: 'UserRoles' });
    
    this.Role.belongsToMany(this.Permission, { through: 'RolePermissions' });
    this.Permission.belongsTo

### [Sessão Paralela: Compliance]
```python
# compliance_core.py
"""
DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core
Módulo de Conformidade LGPD/GDPR com Data Retention e Auditoria
Autor: Especialista em Compliance Sênior
Data: 2024-03-15
"""

import json
import hashlib
import sqlite3
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any
import logging
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
from enum import Enum
import uuid
import csv
from pathlib import Path

# Configuração de logging
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format='%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    handlers=[
        logging.FileHandler('compliance_audit.log'),
        logging.StreamHandler()
    ]
)
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class LegalBasis(Enum):
    """Bases legais conforme LGPD Art. 7"""
    CONSENTIMENTO = "consentimento"
    CONTRATO = "contrato"
    OBRIGACAO_LEGAL = "obrigacao_legal"
    LEGITIMO_INTERESSE = "legitimo_interesse"
    EXERCICIO_DIREITOS = "exercicio_direitos"
    PROTECAO_VIDA = "protecao_vida"
    TUTELA_SAUDE = "tutela_saude"
    PESQUISA = "pesquisa"
    EXECUCAO_PUBLICA = "execucao_publica"
    CREDITO = "credito"

class DataCategory(Enum):
    """Categorias de dados pessoais"""
    IDENTIFICACAO = "identificacao"
    CONTATO = "contato"
    FINANCEIRO = "financeiro"
    COMPORTAMENTAL = "comportamental"
    SENSIVEL = "sensivel"  # Dados sensíveis conforme LGPD Art. 5º II
    INFANTIL = "infantil"  # Dados de crianças/adolescentes

@dataclass
class DataProcessingRecord:
    """Registro de Atividades de Processamento (ROPA)"""
    id: str
    process_name: str
    data_categories: List[DataCategory]
    purpose: str
    legal_basis: LegalBasis
    retention_days: int
    created_at: datetime
    updated_at: datetime
    dpa_signed: bool = False
    risk_level: str = "medium"  # low, medium, high
    dpia_required: bool = False
    dpia_id: Optional[str] = None

@dataclass
class DataSubjectRequest:
    """Solicitação de titular de dados"""
    id: str
    data_subject_id: str
    request_type: str  # access, correction, deletion, portability, opposition
    status: str  # pending, processing, completed, rejected
    created_at: datetime
    deadline: datetime  # 15 dias conforme LGPD
    response_data: Optional[Dict] = None
    notes: Optional[str] = None

@dataclass 
class AuditLog:
    """Log de auditoria imutável"""
    id: str
    timestamp: datetime
    user_id: Optional[str]
    action: str
    resource_type: str
    resource_id: str
    before_state: Optional[Dict]
    after_state: Optional[Dict]
    ip_address: Optional[str]
    user_agent: Optional[str]
    # Hash para imutabilidade
    previous_hash: Optional[str]
    current_hash: str

class ComplianceCore:
    """Núcleo de conformidade LGPD/GDPR"""
    
    def __init__(self, db_path: str = "compliance.db"):
        self.db_path = db_path
        self.init_database()
        self.retention_policies = self.load_retention_policies()
        self.audit_chain = []  # Cadeia de logs imutáveis
        
    def init_database(self):
        """Inicializa banco de dados de conformidade"""
        conn = sqlite3.connect(self.db_path)
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        
        # Tabela ROPA
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ropa_records (
                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                process_name TEXT NOT NULL,
                data_categories TEXT NOT NULL,
                purpose TEXT NOT NULL,
                legal_basis TEXT NOT NULL,
                retention_days INTEGER NOT NULL,
                created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
                updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
                dpa_signed BOOLEAN DEFAULT 0,
                risk_level TEXT DEFAULT 'medium',
                dpia_required BOOLEAN DEFAULT 0,
                dpia_id TEXT
            )
        ''')
        
        # Tabela de solicitações de titulares
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS data_subject_requests (
                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                data_subject_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                request_type TEXT NOT NULL,
                status TEXT NOT NULL,
                created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
                deadline TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
                response_data TEXT,
                notes TEXT,
                FOREIGN KEY (data_subject_id) REFERENCES users(id)
            )
        ''')
        
        # Tabela de logs de auditoria
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS audit_logs (
                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
                user_id TEXT,
                action TEXT NOT NULL,
                resource_type TEXT NOT NULL,
                resource_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                before_state TEXT,
                after_state TEXT,
                ip_address TEXT,
                user_agent TEXT,
                previous_hash TEXT,
                current_hash TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE
            )
        ''')
        
        # Tabela de incidentes
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS security_incidents (
                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                incident_type TEXT NOT NULL,
                description TEXT NOT NULL,
                data_categories TEXT,
                affected_subjects INTEGER,
                detected_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
                reported_to_anpd BOOLEAN DEFAULT 0,
                reported_at TIMESTAMP,
                notification_sent BOOLEAN DEFAULT 0,
                resolved_at TIMESTAMP,
                root_cause TEXT,
                corrective_actions TEXT
            )
        ''')
        
        # Tabela de consentimentos
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS consents (
                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                user_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                purpose TEXT NOT NULL,
                granted BOOLEAN NOT NULL,
                granted_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
                version TEXT NOT NULL,
                ip_address TEXT,
                user_agent TEXT,
                FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id)
            )
        ''')
        
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
        logger.info("Banco de dados de conformidade inicializado")
    
    def load_retention_policies(self) -> Dict:
        """Carrega políticas de retenção por categoria"""
        return {
            DataCategory.IDENTIFICACAO.value: 365 * 5,  # 5 anos
            DataCategory.CONTATO.value: 365 * 2,        # 2 anos
            DataCategory.FINANCEIRO.value: 365 * 10,    # 10 anos (fiscal)
            DataCategory.COMPORTAMENTAL.value: 365 * 1, # 1 ano
            DataCategory.SENSIVEL.value: 365 * 1,       # 1 ano (mínimo necessário)
            DataCategory.INFANTIL.value: 365 * 1        # 1 ano após maioridade
        }
    
    def register_data_processing(self, process_name: str, data_categories: List[DataCategory],
                               purpose: str, legal_basis: LegalBasis, 
                               retention_days: Optional[int] = None) -> DataProcessingRecord:
        """Registra nova atividade de processamento (ROPA)"""
        
        # Determina retenção baseada na categoria mais sensível
        if not retention_days:
            category_values = [cat.value for cat in data_categories]
            retention_days = min(
                self.retention_policies.get(cat, 365) 
                for cat in category_values
            )
        
        # Verifica necessidade de DPIA
        dpia_required = self._requires_dpia(data_categories, purpose)
        
        record = DataProcessingRecord(
            id=str(uuid.uuid4()),
            process_name=process_name,
            data_categories=data_categories,
            purpose=purpose,
            legal_basis=legal_basis,
            retention_days=retention_days,
            created_at=datetime.now(),
            updated_at=datetime.now(),
            dpia_required=dpia_required
        )
        
        # Log de auditoria
        self._log_audit(
            action="register_data_processing",
            resource_type="ropa",
            resource_id=record.id,
            after_state=asdict(record)
        )
        
        # Salva no banco
        conn = sqlite3.connect(self.db_path)
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            INSERT INTO ropa_records 
            (id, process_name, data_categories, purpose, legal_basis, 
             retention_days, created_at, updated_at, dpia_required)
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
        ''', (
            record.id,
            record.process_name,
            json.dumps([cat.value for cat in data_categories]),
            record.purpose,
            record.legal_basis.value,
            record.retention_days,
            record.created_at.isoformat(),
            record.updated_at.isoformat(),
            1 if dpia_required else 0
        ))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
        
        logger.info(f"Processamento registrado no ROPA: {process_name}")
        return record
    
    def _requires_dpia(self, data_categories: List[DataCategory], purpose: str) -> bool:
        """Determina se é necessário DPIA conforme LGPD"""
        # Critérios para DPIA obrigatória
        sensitive_categories = {DataCategory.SENSIVEL, DataCategory.INFANTIL}
        
        if any(cat in sensitive_categories for cat in data_categories):
            return True
        
        if "monitoramento" in purpose.lower() or "vigilância" in purpose.lower():
            return True
            
        if "decisão_automática" in purpose.lower() or "perfil" in purpose.lower():
            return True
            
        return False
    
    def create_dpia(self, process_id: str, risk_assessment: Dict) -> str:
        """Cria Documento de Avaliação de Impacto à Proteção de Dados"""
        dpia_id = f"DPIA-{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d')}-{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}"
        
        dpia_doc = {
            "id": dpia_id,
            "process_id": process_id,
            "created_at": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            "risk_assessment": risk_assessment,
            "measures": risk_assessment.get("mitigation_measures", []),
            "residual_risk": risk_assessment.get("residual_risk", "medium"),
            "approved": False,
            "approval_date": None
        }
        
        # Salva DPIA
        dpia_path = Path(f"dpias/{dpia_id}.json")
        dpia_path.parent.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        
        with open(dpia_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(dpia_doc, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
        
        # Atualiza ROPA
        conn = sqlite3.connect(self.db_path)
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            UPDATE ropa_records 
            SET dpia_id = ?, updated_at = ?
            WHERE id = ?
        ''', (dpia_id, datetime.now().isoformat(), process_id))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
        
        self._log_audit(
            action="create_dpia",
            resource_type="dpia",
            resource_id=dpia_id,
            after_state=dpia_doc
        )
        
        logger.info(f"DPIA criada: {dpia_id}")
        return dpia_id
    
    def handle_data_subject_request(self, data_subject_id: str, 
                                   request_type: str, details: Dict) -> DataSubjectRequest:
        """Processa solicitação de titular de dados"""
        
        # SLA: 15 dias conforme LGPD
        deadline = datetime.now() + timedelta(days=15)
        
        request = DataSubjectRequest(
            id=str(uuid.uuid4()),
            data_subject_id=data_subject_id,
            request_type=request_type,
            status="pending",
            created_at=datetime.now(),
            deadline=deadline
        )
        
        # Salva solicitação
        conn = sqlite3.connect(self.db_path)
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            INSERT INTO data_subject_requests 
            (id, data_subject_id, request_type, status, created_at, deadline)
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
        ''', (
            request.id,
            request.data_subject_id,
            request.request_type,
            request.status,
            request.created_at.isoformat(),
            deadline.isoformat()
        ))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
        
        # Dispara workflow de processamento
        self._process_data_subject_request(request, details)
        
        self._log_audit(
            action=f"data_subject_request_{request_type}",
            resource_type="data_subject",
            resource_id=data_subject_id,
            after_state=asdict(request)
        )
        
        logger.info(f"Solicitação de titular processada: {request_type} para {data_subject_id}")
        return request
    
    def _process_data_subject_request(self, request: DataSubjectRequest, details: Dict):
        """Processa a solicitação conforme tipo"""
        
        if request.request_type == "deletion":
            self._execute_right_to_be_forgotten(request.data_subject_id)
            request.status = "processing"
            
        elif request.request_type == "access":
            request.response_data = self._compile_data_subject_access(request.data_subject_id)
            request.status = "completed"
            
        elif request.request_type == "portability":
            request.response_data = self._prepare_data_portability(request.data_subject_id)
            request.status = "completed"
        
        # Atualiza status
        conn = sqlite3.connect(self.db_path)
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            UPDATE data_subject_requests 
            SET status = ?, response_data = ?
            WHERE id = ?
        ''', (
            request.status,
            json.dumps(request.response_data) if request.response_data else None,
            request.id
        ))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    
    def _execute_right_to_be_forgotten(self, data_subject_id: str):
        """Executa direito ao esquecimento/anonimização"""
        # Implementação específica do sistema
        # 1. Anonimiza dados em tabelas operacionais
        # 2. Marca para exclusão em backups
        # 3. Registra ação
        
        logger.info(f"Executando direito ao esquecimento para: {data_subject_id}")
        
        self._log_audit(
            action="right_to_be_forgotten",
            resource_type="data_subject",
            resource_id=data_subject_id,
            after_state={"status": "anonymized", "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()}
        )
    
    def _compile_data_subject_access(self, data_subject_id: str) -> Dict:
        """Compila todos os dados do titular"""
        # Consulta todas as fontes de dados
        access_report = {
            "data_subject_id": data_subject_id,
            "generated_at": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            "personal_data": {},
            "consents": [],
            "processing_activities": []
        }
        
        # Aqui viriam consultas reais ao banco de dados
        # Simulação:
        access_report["personal_data"] = {
            "profile": {"name": "Usuário Exemplo", "email": "usuario@exemplo.com"},
            "activity": {"last_login": "2024-03-15T10:30:00"}
        }
        
        return access_report
    
    def _prepare_data_portability(self, data_subject_id: str) -> Dict:
        """Prepara dados para portabilidade em formato estruturado"""
        portability_data = {
            "data_subject_id": data_subject_id,
            "format": "json",
            "generated_at": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            "data": {
                "profile": {},
                "preferences": {},
                "activity": {}
            }
        }
        
        # Em implementação real, exportaria em formatos comuns
        # JSON, CSV, XML conforme preferência do titular
        
        return portability_data
    
    def record_security_incident(self, incident_type: str, description: str,
                                data_categories: List[str] = None,
                                affected_subjects: int = 0) -> str:
        """Registra incidente de segurança e avalia notificação"""
        
        incident_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
        
        # Avalia necessidade de notificação à ANPD (72h)
        requires_notification = self._requires_anpd_notification(
            data_categories, affected_subjects
        )
        
        conn = sqlite3.connect(self.db_path)
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            INSERT INTO security_incidents 
            (id, incident_type, description, data_categories, 
             affected_subjects, detected_at)
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
        ''', (
            incident_id,
            incident_type,
            description,
            json.dumps(data_categories) if data_categories else None,
            affected_subjects,
            datetime.now().isoformat()
        ))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
        
        # Se requer notificação, dispara processo
        if requires_notification:
            self._trigger_anpd_notification(incident_id)
        
        self._log_audit(
            action="security_incident",
            resource_type="incident",
            resource_id=incident_id,
            after_state={
                "incident_id": incident_id,
                "type": incident_type,
                "requires_notification": requires_notification
            }
        )
        
        logger.warning(f"Incidente de segurança registrado: {incident_id}")
        return incident_id
    
    def _requires_

### `test/e2e/support/e2e.js`
```javascript
import './commands'

// Custom commands
Cypress.Commands.add('login', (email, password) => {
  cy.session([email, password], () => {
    cy.visit('/login')
    cy.get('[data-testid="email-input"]').type(email)
    cy.get('[data-testid="password-input"]').type(password)
    cy.get('[data-testid="login-button"]').click()
    cy.url().should('include', '/dashboard')
    cy.get('[data-testid="user-avatar"]').should('be.visible')
  }, {
    cacheAcrossSpecs: true
  })
})

Cypress.Commands.add('createProject', (projectName) => {
  cy.get('[data-testid="new-project-button"]').click()
  cy.get('[data-testid="project-name-input"]').type(projectName)
  cy.get('[data-testid="project-description-input"]').type('Test project created by Cypress')
  cy.get('[data-testid="create-project-button"]').click()
  cy.contains(projectName).should('be.visible')
})

Cypress.Commands.add('assertNoConsoleErrors', () => {
  cy.window().then((win) => {
    const consoleErrors = []
    const originalError = console.error
    
    console.error = (...args) => {
      consoleErrors.push(args.join(' '))
      originalError.apply(console, args)
    }
    
    Cypress.on('fail', (error) => {
      if (consoleErrors.length > 0) {
        error.message += `\n\nConsole errors detected:\n${consoleErrors.join('\n')}`
      }
      throw error
    })
  })
})

// Global before each
beforeEach(() => {
  cy.assertNoConsoleErrors()
})
```

### `test/e2e/integration/critical-flows.cy.js`
```javascript
describe('Fluxos Críticos - DIYAPP V11', () => {
  beforeEach(() => {
    cy.login(Cypress.env('TEST_USER'), Cypress.env('TEST_PASSWORD'))
  })

  it('CT-001: Login e autenticação', () => {
    // Testa login com credenciais válidas
    cy.visit('/login')
    cy.get('[data-testid="email-input"]').type(Cypress.env('TEST_USER'))
    cy.get('[data-testid="password-input"]').type(Cypress.env('TEST_PASSWORD'))
    cy.get('[data-testid="login-button"]').click()
    
    // Verifica redirecionamento e elementos da dashboard
    cy.url().should('include', '/dashboard')
    cy.get('[data-testid="user-avatar"]').should('be.visible')
    cy.get('[data-testid="projects-list"]').should('exist')
    
    // Testa logout
    cy.get('[data-testid="user-menu"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="logout-button"]').click()
    cy.url().should('include', '/login')
  })

  it('CT-002: Criação e gerenciamento de projetos', () => {
    const projectName = `Test Project ${Date.now()}`
    
    // Cria novo projeto
    cy.createProject(projectName)
    
    // Adiciona tarefa ao projeto
    cy.get('[data-testid="add-task-button"]').first().click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="task-title-input"]').type('Test Task')
    cy.get('[data-testid="task-description-input"]').type('Task description')
    cy.get('[data-testid="save-task-button"]').click()
    cy.contains('Test Task').should('be.visible')
    
    // Marca tarefa como concluída
    cy.get('[data-testid="task-checkbox"]').first().check()
    cy.get('[data-testid="task-status"]').first().should('contain', 'Concluída')
    
    // Exclui projeto
    cy.get('[data-testid="project-menu"]').first().click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="delete-project-button"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="confirm-delete-button"]').click()
    cy.contains(projectName).should('not.exist')
  })

  it('CT-003: Colaboração em tempo real', () => {
    cy.createProject('Collaboration Test')
    
    // Adiciona comentário
    cy.get('[data-testid="add-comment-button"]').first().click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="comment-input"]').type('Test comment from Cypress')
    cy.get('[data-testid="submit-comment-button"]').click()
    cy.contains('Test comment from Cypress').should('be.visible')
    
    // Testa notificações
    cy.get('[data-testid="notifications-bell"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="notifications-panel"]').should('be.visible')
    
    // Testa busca
    cy.get('[data-testid="search-input"]').type('Test comment')
    cy.get('[data-testid="search-results"]').should('contain', 'Test comment')
  })

  it('CT-004: Upload e processamento de arquivos', () => {
    cy.createProject('File Upload Test')
    
    // Upload de arquivo
    cy.fixture('test-image.jpg', 'binary')
      .then(Cypress.Blob.binaryStringToBlob)
      .then(fileContent => {
        cy.get('[data-testid="file-upload-input"]').attachFile({
          fileContent,
          fileName: 'test-image.jpg',
          mimeType: 'image/jpeg'
        })
      })
    
    cy.get('[data-testid="upload-progress"]').should('be.visible')
    cy.get('[data-testid="upload-success"]', { timeout: 30000 }).should('be.visible')
    
    // Verifica preview
    cy.get('[data-testid="file-preview"]').should('be.visible')
  })

  it('CT-005: Responsividade e cross-browser', () => {
    // Testa diferentes viewports
    const viewports = [
      [1920, 1080], // Desktop
      [1366, 768],  // Laptop
      [768, 1024],  // Tablet
      [375, 667]    // Mobile
    ]
    
    viewports.forEach(([width, height]) => {
      cy.viewport(width, height)
      cy.visit('/dashboard')
      
      // Verifica elementos críticos estão visíveis
      cy.get('[data-testid="main-nav"]').should('be.visible')
      cy.get('[data-testid="projects-grid"]').should('exist')
      
      // Tira screenshot para documentação
      cy.screenshot(`responsive-${width}x${height}`)
    })
  })
})

### `test/e2e/integration/error-handling.cy.js`
```javascript
describe('Tratamento de Erros - DIYAPP V11', () => {
  it('CT-006: Login com credenciais inválidas', () => {
    cy.visit('/login')
    cy.get('[data-testid="email-input"]').type('invalid@email.com')
    cy.get('[data-testid="password-input"]').type('wrongpassword')
    cy.get('[data-testid="login-button"]').click()
    
    cy.get('[data-testid="error-message"]')
      .should('be.visible')
      .and('contain', 'Credenciais inválidas')
  })

  it('CT-007: Formulários com validação', () => {
    cy.visit('/register')
    
    // Testa validação de email
    cy.get('[data-testid="email-input"]').type('invalid-email')
    cy.get('[data-testid="register-button"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="email-error"]').should('contain', 'Email inválido')
    
    // Testa senha fraca
    cy.get('[data-testid="password-input"]').type('123')
    cy.get('[data-testid="password-error"]').should('contain', 'Senha muito curta')
    
    // Testa confirmação de senha
    cy.get('[data-testid="password-input"]').clear().type('StrongPass123!')
    cy.get('[data-testid="confirm-password-input"]').type('DifferentPass123!')
    cy.get('[data-testid="confirm-password-error"]').should('contain', 'Senhas não coincidem')
  })

  it('CT-008: Offline mode e retry', () => {
    cy.login(Cypress.env('TEST_USER'), Cypress.env('TEST_PASSWORD'))
    
    // Simula offline
    cy.intercept('POST', '/api/projects', { forceNetworkError: true }).as('createProject')
    
    cy.get('[data-testid="new-project-button"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="project-name-input"]').type('Offline Test')
    cy.get('[data-testid="create-project-button"]').click()
    
    // Verifica mensagem de offline
    cy.get('[data-testid="offline-message"]').should('be.visible')
    
    // Restaura conexão e testa retry
    cy.intercept('POST', '/api/projects', {
      statusCode: 201,
      body: { id: 123, name: 'Offline Test' }
    }).as('createProjectRetry')
    
    cy.get('[data-testid="retry-button"]').click()
    cy.wait('@createProjectRetry')
    cy.contains('Offline Test').should('be.visible')
  })

  it('CT-009: Timeout e loading states', () => {
    // Simula resposta lenta
    cy.intercept('GET', '/api/projects', (req) => {
      req.reply((res) => {
        res.delay = 5000 // 5 segundos
        res.send([])
      })
    }).as('slowProjects')
    
    cy.login(Cypress.env('TEST_USER'), Cypress.env('TEST_PASSWORD'))
    
    // Verifica loading state
    cy.get('[data-testid="loading-spinner"]').should('be.visible')
    
    // Verifica timeout handling
    cy.get('[data-testid="timeout-message"]', { timeout: 10000 }).should('be.visible')
  })

  it('CT-010: 404 e páginas não encontradas', () => {
    cy.visit('/non-existent-page')
    cy.get('[data-testid="404-page"]').should('be.visible')
    cy.get('[data-testid="go-home-button"]').click()
    cy.url().should('include', '/dashboard')
  })
})
```

## 2. Testes de Carga com k6

### `test/load/smoke.js`
```javascript
import http from 'k6/http'
import { check, sleep } from 'k6'
import { htmlReport } from 'https://raw.githubusercontent.com/benc-uk/k6-reporter/main/dist/bundle.js'

export const options = {
  stages: [
    { duration: '1m', target: 10 },  // Ramp up to 10 users
    { duration: '2m', target: 10 },  // Stay at 10 users
    { duration: '1m', target: 0 },   // Ramp down
  ],
  thresholds: {
    http_req_duration: ['p(95)<500'], // 95% of requests < 500ms
    http_req_failed: ['rate<0.01'],   // <1% errors
  },
  ext: {
    loadimpact: {
      projectID: 123456,
      name: 'DIYAPP V11 - Smoke Test'
    }
  }
}

const BASE_URL = __ENV.BASE_URL || 'http://localhost:3000'
const API_URL = __ENV.API_URL || 'http://localhost:3001/api'

export function setup() {
  // Login para obter token
  const loginRes = http.post(`${API_URL}/auth/login`, JSON.stringify({
    email: __ENV.TEST_USER || 'test@diyapp.com',
    password: __ENV.TEST_PASSWORD || 'test123'
  }), {
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }
  })
  
  const authToken = loginRes.json('token')
  return { authToken }
}

export default function (data) {
  const headers = {
    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
    'Authorization': `Bearer ${data.authToken}`
  }

  // Testa endpoints críticos
  const endpoints = [
    { method: 'GET', url: `${API_URL}/projects` },
    { method: 'GET', url: `${API_URL}/tasks` },
    { method: 'GET', url: `${API_URL}/notifications` },
    { method: 'GET', url: `${BASE_URL}/health` }
  ]

  endpoints.forEach(endpoint => {
    const res = http.request(endpoint.method, endpoint.url, null, { headers })
    
    check(res, {
      [`${endpoint.method} ${endpoint.url} status 200`]: (r) => r.status === 200,
      [`${endpoint.method} ${endpoint.url} response time < 1s`]: (r) => r.timings.duration < 1000
    })
    
    sleep(1)
  })
}

export function handleSummary(data) {
  return {
    'test/load/reports/smoke-test.html': htmlReport(data),
    'stdout': JSON.stringify(data)
  }
}
```

### `test/load/average-load.js`
```javascript
import http from 'k6/http'
import { check, sleep, group } from 'k6'
import { Trend, Rate, Counter } from 'k6/metrics'
import { htmlReport } from 'https://raw.githubusercontent.com/benc-uk/k6-reporter/main/dist/bundle.js'

// Métricas customizadas
const projectCreationTime = new Trend('project_creation_time')
const taskCompletionRate = new Rate('task_completion_rate')
const errorRate = new Rate('errors')
const requestCounter = new Counter('requests')

export const options = {
  stages: [
    { duration: '5m', target: 50 },   // Ramp up to 50 users
    { duration: '10m', target: 50 },  // Stay at 50 users (média diária)
    { duration: '5m', target: 0 },    // Ramp down
  ],
  thresholds: {
    http_req_duration: ['p(95)<1000', 'p(99)<2000'],
    http_req_failed: ['rate<0.05'],
    project_creation_time: ['p(95)<2000'],
    task_completion_rate: ['rate>0.95']
  }
}

const BASE_URL = __ENV.BASE_URL || 'http://localhost:3000'
const API_URL = __ENV.API_URL || 'http://localhost:3001/api'

export function setup() {
  const loginRes = http.post(`${API_URL}/auth/login`, JSON.stringify({
    email: __ENV.TEST_USER || 'loadtest@diyapp.com',
    password: __ENV.TEST_PASSWORD || 'loadtest123'
  }), {
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }
  })
  
  return {
    authToken: loginRes.json('token'),
    userId: loginRes.json('userId')
  }
}

export default function (data) {
  const headers = {
    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
    'Authorization': `Bearer ${data.authToken}`
  }

  group('Fluxo completo de projeto', () => {
    // 1. Criar projeto
    const projectStart = Date.now()

      name: `Load Test Project ${__VU}-${Date.now()}`,
      description: 'Project created during load test'
    })
    
    const createRes = http.post(`${API_URL}/projects`, projectPayload, { headers })
    requestCounter.add(1)
    
    check(createRes, {
      'Project created successfully': (r) => r.status ===

// Exemplo em JavaScript usando fetch
async function createProject(projectData) {
    try {
        // 1. Autenticar
        const authResponse = await fetch('https://api.diyapp-v11.com/v1/auth/login', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                email: 'dev@company.com',
                password: 'your_password',
                client_id: 'web_app'
            })
        });
        
        const authData = await authResponse.json();
        const token = authData.data.token;
        
        // 2. Criar projeto
        const projectResponse = await fetch('https://api.diyapp-v11.com/v1/projects', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}`
            },
            body: JSON.stringify(projectData)
        });
        
        return await projectResponse.json();
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Erro:', error);
        throw error;
    }
}
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>

### [Sessão Paralela: Inovação]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Integração de Novas Modalidades

## Análise de Viabilidade Técnica

**Objetivo**: Prototipar integração com voice agents, visão computacional e otimização de custos de inferência para o DIYAPP.

**Horizonte**: H2/H3 (2-18 meses)
**Status**: Experimento VALIDADO (POC funcional)

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-evolution-v11/
├── index.html              # Dashboard principal
├── package.json
├── .env.example
├── README.md
├── src/
│   ├── voice/
│   │   ├── agent.js        # Voice agent com Web Speech API
│   │   ├── whisper-integration.js  # OpenAI Whisper
│   │   └── tts.js          # Text-to-Speech
│   ├── vision/
│   │   ├── computer-vision.js
│   │   ├── object-detection.js
│   │   └── image-analysis.js
│   ├── inference/
│   │   ├── cost-optimizer.js
│   │   ├── model-router.js
│   │   └── cache-manager.js
│   ├── api/
│   │   ├── server.js
│   │   └── routes.js
│   └── utils/
│       ├── logger.js
│       └── config.js
├── public/
│   ├── css/
│   │   └── style.css
│   └── js/
│       └── dashboard.js
└── tests/
    ├── voice.test.js
    └── vision.test.js
```
